# GEMINI_API_KEY: Required for Gemini AI API calls.
# AI Studio automatically injects this at runtime from user secrets.
# Users configure this via the Secrets panel in the AI Studio UI.
GEMINI_API_KEY="MY_GEMINI_API_KEY"

# APP_URL: The URL where this applet is hosted.
# AI Studio automatically injects this at runtime with the Cloud Run service URL.
# Used for self-referential links, OAuth callbacks, and API endpoints.
APP_URL="MY_APP_URL"

# Run and deploy your AI Studio app

This contains everything you need to run your app locally.

View your app in AI Studio: https://ai.studio/apps/6cf48f55-9a55-42f9-9171-c26885c21d09

## Run Locally

**Prerequisites:**  Node.js


1. Install dependencies:
   `npm install`
2. Set the `GEMINI_API_KEY` in [.env.local](.env.local) to your Gemini API key
3. Run the app:
   `npm run dev`

// Touch Tools Bootstrapper for users running 'node server.js' directly
const { spawn } = require("child_process");
const path = require("path");

console.log("==================================================");
console.log("  Touch Tools Proxy Bootstrapper Active");
console.log("  Redirecting 'node server.js' -> 'npx tsx server.ts'");
console.log("==================================================");

const child = spawn("npx", ["tsx", "server.ts"], {
  cwd: __dirname,
  stdio: "inherit",
  shell: true
});

child.on("exit", (code) => {
  process.exit(code || 0);
});


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: server.ts
------------------------------------------------------------

import express from "express";
import http from "http";
import net from "net";
import path from "path";
import fs from "fs";
import { execFile } from "child_process";
import { WebSocket, WebSocketServer } from "ws";
import { createServer as createViteServer } from "vite";

const HTTP_PORT = 3000; // AI Studio routes ONLY port 3000 to external
const TCP_PORT = 8092;  // Standard After Effects jsx hub port

// --- TOUCHTOOLS SYSTEM DIAGNOSTIC RUNTIME ENGNE ---
interface DiagnosticReport {
  sessionStart: string;
  sessionEnd?: string;
  nodeVersion: string;
  platform: string;
  arch: string;
  cwd: string;
  aePathConfigured: string;
  files: {
    packageJson: boolean;
    bridgeJsx: boolean;
    configJson: boolean;
    startBat: boolean;
  };
  metrics: {
    browserWebSocketConnectionsCount: number;
    aeTcpConnectionsCount: number;
    commandsReceivedFromBrowser: number;
    commandsSentToAE: number;
    commandsResolved: number;
    commandsFailed: number;
    commandsTimedOut: number;
  };
  errors: Array<{
    timestamp: string;
    type: "websocket" | "tcp" | "ae_script" | "parse" | "server";
    message: string;
    details?: string;
    count: number;
  }>;
}

const diagnostics: DiagnosticReport = {
  sessionStart: new Date().toISOString(),
  nodeVersion: process.version,
  platform: process.platform,
  arch: process.arch,
  cwd: process.cwd(),
  aePathConfigured: "",
  files: {
    packageJson: fs.existsSync("package.json"),
    bridgeJsx: fs.existsSync("bridge.jsx"),
    configJson: fs.existsSync("config.json"),
    startBat: fs.existsSync("start-touchtools.bat")
  },
  metrics: {
    browserWebSocketConnectionsCount: 0,
    aeTcpConnectionsCount: 0,
    commandsReceivedFromBrowser: 0,
    commandsSentToAE: 0,
    commandsResolved: 0,
    commandsFailed: 0,
    commandsTimedOut: 0
  },
  errors: []
};

function saveDiagnostics() {
  try {
    diagnostics.files.bridgeJsx = fs.existsSync("bridge.jsx");
    diagnostics.files.configJson = fs.existsSync("config.json");
    
    fs.writeFileSync(
      path.join(process.cwd(), "touchtools-diagnostics.json"),
      JSON.stringify(diagnostics, null, 2),
      "utf8"
    );
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("Failed to write JSON diagnostics snapshot:", err.message);
  }
}

function logDiagnosticError(type: "websocket" | "tcp" | "ae_script" | "parse" | "server", message: string, details?: string) {
  const existing = diagnostics.errors.find(e => e.type === type && e.message === message);
  if (existing) {
    existing.count++;
    existing.timestamp = new Date().toISOString();
  } else {
    diagnostics.errors.push({
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      type,
      message,
      details,
      count: 1
    });
  }
  saveDiagnostics();
}

function writeDiagnosticReport(sessionFinished: boolean = false) {
  if (sessionFinished) {
    diagnostics.sessionEnd = new Date().toISOString();
  }
  saveDiagnostics();
  
  try {
    let logText = `==================================================\n`;
    logText += `        TOUCHTOOLS SYSTEM DIAGNOSTIC LOG          \n`;
    logText += `==================================================\n`;
    logText += `Report Generated: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}\n`;
    logText += `Session Start:    ${new Date(diagnostics.sessionStart).toLocaleString()}\n`;
    if (sessionFinished && diagnostics.sessionEnd) {
      logText += `Session End:      ${new Date(diagnostics.sessionEnd).toLocaleString()}\n\n`;
    } else {
      logText += `Session End:      STILL ACTIVE / CURRENTLY RUNNING\n\n`;
    }
    logText += `SYSTEM ENVIRONMENT:\n`;
    logText += `- Node.js Version: ${diagnostics.nodeVersion}\n`;
    logText += `- OS Platform:     ${diagnostics.platform} (${diagnostics.arch})\n`;
    logText += `- Directory:       ${diagnostics.cwd}\n`;
    logText += `- AE Config Path:  ${diagnostics.aePathConfigured || "Not configured"}\n\n`;
    
    logText += `FILES INTEGRITY CHECK:\n`;
    logText += `- package.json:      ${diagnostics.files.packageJson ? "FOUND [OK]" : "MISSING [WARNING]"}\n`;
    logText += `- bridge.jsx:        ${diagnostics.files.bridgeJsx ? "FOUND [OK]" : "MISSING [CRITICAL]"}\n`;
    logText += `- config.json:       ${diagnostics.files.configJson ? "FOUND [OK]" : "NOT REGISTERED YET"}\n\n`;
    
    logText += `COMMUNICATION METRICS:\n`;
    logText += `- Unique browser WS handshakes: ${diagnostics.metrics.browserWebSocketConnectionsCount}\n`;
    logText += `- After Effects TCP handshakes: ${diagnostics.metrics.aeTcpConnectionsCount}\n`;
    logText += `- Browser commands received:    ${diagnostics.metrics.commandsReceivedFromBrowser}\n`;
    logText += `- Bridge commands sent:         ${diagnostics.metrics.commandsSentToAE}\n`;
    logText += `- Commands successfully run:    ${diagnostics.metrics.commandsResolved}\n`;
    logText += `- Commands errored/failed:      ${diagnostics.metrics.commandsFailed}\n`;
    logText += `- Commands timeout occurrences: ${diagnostics.metrics.commandsTimedOut}\n\n`;
    
    logText += `UNIQUE SYSTEM ERRORS LOGGED (DEDUPLICATED):\n`;
    if (diagnostics.errors.length === 0) {
      logText += `[PASS] Zero runtime errors registered during this active session!\n`;
    } else {
      diagnostics.errors.forEach((err, idx) => {
        logText += `${idx + 1}. [${err.timestamp}] (${err.type.toUpperCase()}) (Seen ${err.count} times):\n`;
        logText += `   Error Msg: ${err.message}\n`;
        if (err.details) {
          logText += `   Details:   ${err.details}\n`;
        }
      });
    }
    
    logText += `\n==================================================\n`;
    logText += `      DIAGNOSTIC ADVISORY GUIDE & RESOLUTIONS\n`;
    logText += `==================================================\n`;
    logText += `1. AFTER EFFECTS LAGGING / FREEZING?\n`;
    logText += `   - RESOLVED: The newest Bridge.jsx script uses non-blocking polling scheduled tasks.\n`;
    logText += `     Ensure you are running the latest bridge.jsx exported in this directory!\n`;
    logText += `     The script will never retry connecting too aggressively if the server drops.\n\n`;
    logText += `2. NO RESPONSE IN BROWSER COMPONENT WORKSPACE?\n`;
    logText += `   - Ensure 'bridge.jsx' is active in After Effects (File > Scripts > Run Script File...).\n`;
    logText += `     Check that preferences are set to allow access to network under Preferences > Expressions.\n\n`;
    logText += `3. HOW TO SHARE METADATA LOGS?\n`;
    logText += `   - Simply send or upload 'touchtools-diagnostics.json' or 'touchtools-diagnostics.log'\n`;
    logText += `     to your AI assistant for seamless automated code patch generation!\n`;
    logText += `==================================================\n`;
    
    fs.writeFileSync(path.join(process.cwd(), "touchtools-diagnostics.log"), logText, "utf8");
  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error("Failed to write human-readable diagnostics:", err.message);
  }
}

function quitGracefully() {
  writeDiagnosticReport(true);
}

// Ensure signal registers
process.on("SIGINT", () => {
  console.log("\n[SHUTDOWN] Exiting gracefully, dumping system session diagnostic log...");
  quitGracefully();
  process.exit(0);
});

process.on("SIGTERM", () => {
  quitGracefully();
  process.exit(0);
});

// Define the full bridge.jsx script in the source code to guarantee it's auto-generated on launch
const BRIDGE_JSX_CONTENT = `/**
 * AFTER EFFECTS TO TOUCHTOOLS TCP BRIDGE SCRIPT (NON-BLOCKING)
 * 
 * Instructions:
 * 1. Open Adobe After Effects.
 * 2. Ensure "Allow Scripts to Write Files and Access Network" is enabled:
 *    Preferences > Scripting & Expressions > Check "Allow Scripts to Write Files and Access Network"
 * 3. Go to File > Scripts > Run Script File... and choose this bridge.jsx.
 * 4. This runs in the background (non-blocking). After Effects remains fully active and interactive!
 */

var TouchToolsBridge = {
    host: "127.0.0.1",
    port: 8092,
     socket: null,
    taskId: null,
    buffer: "",
    isActive: false,
    lastConnectAttempt: 0,
    isOpen: false, // Explicit connection state tracking flag since ExtendScript Socket lacks 'connected' property
    
    connect: function() {
        if (this.socket) {
            try { this.socket.close(); } catch(e) {}
        }
        
        var s = new Socket();
        s.timeout = 0; // Set socket timeout to 0 (non-blocking)
        
        $.writeln("TouchTools: Connecting to " + this.host + ":" + this.port + "...");
        
        if (!s.open(this.host + ":" + this.port, "UTF-8")) {
            $.writeln("TouchTools: Handshake connection failed. Standby mode active.");
            this.isOpen = false;
            return false;
        }
        
        this.socket = s;
        this.socket.timeout = 0; // ensure non-blocking read
        this.isOpen = true;
        
        $.writeln("TouchTools: Connected successfully!");
        
        // Handshake
        this.socket.write(JSON.stringify({
            type: "status",
            status: "connected",
            message: "After Effects is hooked up and ready"
        }) + "\\n");
        
        this.buffer = "";
        return true;
    },
    
    poll: function() {
        // Auto-reconnect if socket drops - throttled to every 5000ms to preserve After Effects performance!
        if (!this.isOpen || !this.socket) {
            var now = new Date().getTime();
            if (now - this.lastConnectAttempt < 5000) {
                return; // Delay retry so we do not freeze After Effects
            }
            this.lastConnectAttempt = now;
            $.writeln("TouchTools: Socket offline. Reconnecting...");
            if (!this.connect()) {
                return;
            }
        }
        
        try {
            if (this.socket.connected === false) {
                throw new Error("closed");
            }

            // Direct immediate read of any waiting buffer characters (non-blocking)
            var data = this.socket.read();
            
            // Check for termination / empty responses and actual closed signals
            if (data === null || data === "") {
                // On some systems socket.read() returns "" or null when empty but still connected.
                // We verify socket health with write("") fallback and the connected property.
                if (this.socket.connected === false) {
                    throw new Error("closed");
                }
                try {
                    this.socket.write("");
                    if (this.socket.error && this.socket.error.indexOf("closed") !== -1) {
                        throw new Error("closed");
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                    throw new Error("closed");
                }
            } else if (this.socket.error && this.socket.error.indexOf("closed") !== -1) {
                throw new Error("closed");
            }
            
            if (data && data.length > 0) {
                this.buffer += data;
                var lines = this.buffer.split("\\n");
                this.buffer = lines.pop(); // save incomplete line
                
                for (var i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
                    var line = lines[i].replace(/^\\s+|\\s+$/g, '');
                    if (line === '') continue;
                    
                    try {
                        var cmd = JSON.parse(line);
                        this.handleCommand(cmd);
                    } catch (e) {
                        $.writeln("TouchTools: JSON parse/exec error: " + e.toString());
                    }
                }
            }
        } catch (err) {
            $.writeln("TouchTools: Read error: " + err.toString());
            this.isOpen = false;
            try { this.socket.close(); } catch (e) {}
            this.socket = null;
        }
    },
    
    handleCommand: function(cmd) {
        if (!cmd.id) return;
        
        var resultStr = "";
        var isError = false;
        
        try {
            if (cmd.action === "executeScript") {
                var value = eval(cmd.script);
                resultStr = value !== undefined ? String(value) : "undefined";
            } else if (cmd.action === "addSolid") {
                var activeComp = app.project.activeItem;
                if (activeComp && activeComp instanceof CompItem) {
                    var layer = activeComp.layers.addSolid(
                        cmd.color || [1, 1, 1],
                        cmd.name || "Solid Layer",
                        cmd.width || activeComp.width,
                        cmd.height || activeComp.height,
                        activeComp.pixelAspect,
                        activeComp.duration
                    );
                    resultStr = "Created solid layer: " + layer.name;
                } else {
                    throw new Error("No active composition found selection.");
                }
            } else if (cmd.action === "addText") {
                var activeComp = app.project.activeItem;
                if (activeComp && activeComp instanceof CompItem) {
                    var layer = activeComp.layers.addText(cmd.text || "TouchTools Text");
                    resultStr = "Created text layer: " + layer.name;
                } else {
                    throw new Error("No active composition found selection.");
                }
            } else if (cmd.action === "addShape") {
                var activeComp = app.project.activeItem;
                if (activeComp && activeComp instanceof CompItem) {
                    var layer = activeComp.layers.addShape();
                    layer.name = cmd.name || "Shape Layer";
                    resultStr = "Created shape layer: " + layer.name;
                } else {
                    throw new Error("No active composition found.");
                }
            } else if (cmd.action === "updateTransform") {
                var activeComp = app.project.activeItem;
                if (activeComp && activeComp instanceof CompItem) {
                    var layer = activeComp.layer(cmd.layerIndex);
                    if (layer) {
                        if (cmd.position) {
                            layer.property("ADBE Transform Group").property("ADBE Position").setValue(cmd.position);
                        }
                        if (cmd.scale) {
                            layer.property("ADBE Transform Group").property("ADBE Scale").setValue([cmd.scale, cmd.scale, 100]);
                        }
                        if (cmd.opacity !== undefined) {
                            layer.property("ADBE Transform Group").property("ADBE Opacity").setValue(cmd.opacity);
                        }
                        resultStr = "Updated layer properties";
                    } else {
                        throw new Error("Layer not found at index: " + cmd.layerIndex);
                    }
                } else {
                    throw new Error("No active composition found.");
                }
            } else if (cmd.action === "setValue") {
                // EXTREMELY IMPORTANT: direct property values from interactive slider components
                var activeComp = app.project.activeItem;
                if (activeComp && activeComp instanceof CompItem) {
                    var layer = activeComp.layer(cmd.layerIndex);
                    if (layer) {
                        var prop = layer;
                        if (cmd.propertyGroup) {
                            prop = prop.property(cmd.propertyGroup);
                        }
                        if (prop && cmd.propertyPath) {
                            prop = prop.property(cmd.propertyPath);
                        }
                        if (prop && typeof prop.setValue === "function") {
                            prop.setValue(cmd.value);
                            resultStr = "Set property value successfully";
                        } else {
                            throw new Error("Property path not settable or missing");
                        }
                    } else {
                        throw new Error("Layer not found at index: " + cmd.layerIndex);
                    }
                } else {
                    throw new Error("No active composition found.");
                }
            } else {
                throw new Error("Unknown action: " + cmd.action);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            resultStr = e.toString();
            isError = true;
        }
        
        var response = {
            id: cmd.id,
            type: isError ? "error" : "result",
            result: isError ? null : resultStr,
            error: isError ? resultStr : null
        };
        
        try {
            this.socket.write(JSON.stringify(response) + "\\n");
            if (this.socket.error) {
                $.writeln("TouchTools: Write error registered: " + this.socket.error);
                this.isOpen = false;
            }
        } catch (err) {
            $.writeln("TouchTools: Write response failed: " + err.toString());
            this.isOpen = false;
        }
    },
    
    stop: function() {
        if (this.taskId) {
            try { app.cancelTask(this.taskId); } catch(e) {}
            this.taskId = null;
        }
        if (this.socket) {
            try { this.socket.close(); } catch(e) {}
            this.socket = null;
        }
        this.isActive = false;
        $.writeln("TouchTools: Background Scheduler Cleared.");
    },
    
    start: function() {
        this.stop();
        this.connect();
        this.isActive = true;
        // Schedule poll checks every 40ms without freezing After Effects!
        this.taskId = app.scheduleTask("TouchToolsBridge.poll();", 40, true);
        $.writeln("TouchTools: Non-blocking client started in background container.");
    }
};

// Simple, syntax-error free JSON Shim for older ExtendScript contexts
if (typeof JSON !== "object") {
    JSON = {
        parse: function(str) { return eval("(" + str + ")"); },
        stringify: function(obj) {
            var t = typeof (obj);
            if (t !== "object" || obj === null) {
                if (t === "string") return '"' + obj.replace(/"/g, '\\\\"') + '"';
                return String(obj);
            } else {
                var json = [], arr = (obj && obj.constructor === Array);
                for (var n in obj) {
                    var v = obj[n], vt = typeof(v);
                    if (vt === "string") v = '"' + v.replace(/"/g, '\\\\"') + '"';
                    else if (vt === "object" && v !== null) v = JSON.stringify(v);
                    json.push((arr ? "" : '"' + n + '":') + String(v));
                }
                return (arr ? "[" : "{") + String(json) + (arr ? "]" : "}");
            }
        }
    };
}

TouchToolsBridge.start();
`;

// Unconditionally write out the bridge.jsx script to current working directory so it is ALWAYS available!
const bridgeJsxPath = path.join(process.cwd(), "bridge.jsx");
fs.writeFileSync(bridgeJsxPath, BRIDGE_JSX_CONTENT, "utf8");
console.log(`[INIT] Auto-generated bridge.jsx at: ${bridgeJsxPath}`);

const CONFIG_PATH = path.join(process.cwd(), "config.json");
let config = { aePath: "" };
if (fs.existsSync(CONFIG_PATH)) {
  try {
    config = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(CONFIG_PATH, "utf8"));
  } catch (e: any) {
    console.error("Error reading config.json:", e);
    logDiagnosticError("server", "Error loading config.json", e.message);
  }
}

// Persist the starting diagnostics snapshot
diagnostics.aePathConfigured = config.aePath;
writeDiagnosticReport(false);

async function startServer() {
  const app = express();
  app.use(express.json());

  // API Endpoints
  app.get("/api/status", (req, res) => {
    res.json({
      server: true,
      bridge: bridgeSocket !== null && !bridgeSocket.destroyed,
      aePath: config.aePath
    });
  });

  app.get("/api/diagnostics", (req, res) => {
    res.json(diagnostics);
  });

  app.get("/api/download-bridge", (req, res) => {
    const filePath = path.join(process.cwd(), "bridge.jsx");
    if (fs.existsSync(filePath)) {
      res.setHeader("Content-Disposition", "attachment; filename=bridge.jsx");
      res.setHeader("Content-Type", "application/javascript");
      res.sendFile(filePath);
    } else {
      res.status(404).send("bridge.jsx file not found on the server filesystem.");
    }
  });

  app.post("/api/config", (req, res) => {
    if (req.body.aePath !== undefined) {
      config.aePath = req.body.aePath;
    }
    try {
      fs.writeFileSync(CONFIG_PATH, JSON.stringify(config, null, 2));
      diagnostics.aePathConfigured = config.aePath;
      saveDiagnostics();
      res.json({ ok: true });
    } catch(e: any) {
      logDiagnosticError("server", "Failed to write config to system", e.message);
      res.status(500).json({ error: "Failed to write config: " + e.message });
    }
  });

  app.post("/api/launch-bridge", (req, res) => {
    if (!config.aePath || !fs.existsSync(config.aePath)) {
      logDiagnosticError("server", "Failed to launch After Effects - path invalid or missing file", config.aePath || "empty");
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "After Effects path not set or invalid on server filesystem" });
    }
    // Launch AE with bridge script option
    execFile(config.aePath, ["-r", path.join(process.cwd(), "bridge.jsx")], (err) => {
      if (err) {
        console.log("AE launch trigger log:", err.message);
        logDiagnosticError("server", "After Effects executable launch failure", err.message);
      }
    });
    res.json({ ok: true, message: "Bridge launch command sent" });
  });

  const httpServer = http.createServer(app);

  // WebSocket Server on port 3000 (same port as HTTP)
  const wss = new WebSocketServer({ server: httpServer });
  let browserClients: WebSocket[] = [];

  wss.on("connection", (ws, req) => {
    browserClients.push(ws);
    diagnostics.metrics.browserWebSocketConnectionsCount++;
    saveDiagnostics();
    console.log(`[WS] Browser connected from ${req.socket.remoteAddress} (${browserClients.length} total)`);
    
    // Send immediate connection status
    ws.send(JSON.stringify({ 
      type: "bridge_status", 
      connected: bridgeSocket !== null && !bridgeSocket.destroyed 
    }));

    ws.on("message", (raw) => {
      diagnostics.metrics.commandsReceivedFromBrowser++;
      try {
        const msg = JSON.parse(raw.toString());
        handleBrowserMessage(ws, msg);
      } catch (e: any) {
        console.error("[WS] Parse error:", e.message);
        logDiagnosticError("parse", "Unable to parse incoming web client message JSON payload", e.message);
      }
    });

    ws.on("close", () => {
      browserClients = browserClients.filter(c => c !== ws);
      console.log(`[WS] Browser disconnected (${browserClients.length} remaining)`);
    });

    ws.on("error", (err) => {
      console.error("[WS] Client socket error:", err.message);
      logDiagnosticError("websocket", "Client websocket connection encountered an error", err.message);
    });
  });

  function broadcastToBrowsers(obj: any) {
    const data = JSON.stringify(obj);
    browserClients.forEach(ws => {
      if (ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
        ws.send(data);
      }
    });
  }

  interface PendingCommand {
    ws: WebSocket;
    ts: number;
  }

  const pendingCommands: { [key: string]: PendingCommand } = {};

  function handleBrowserMessage(ws: WebSocket, msg: any) {
    if (msg.action === "sendToAE") {
      const cmd = msg.command;
      if (!cmd || !cmd.id) return;

      if (bridgeSocket === null || bridgeSocket.destroyed) {
        logDiagnosticError("ae_script", "Failed browser command sending - bridge not hooked up", "After Effects bridge not active. Run bridge.jsx");
        ws.send(JSON.stringify({ 
          type: "error", 
          id: cmd.id, 
          error: "After Effects bridge not connected. Ensure After Effects is open and running bridge.jsx." 
        }));
        return;
      }
      
      diagnostics.metrics.commandsSentToAE++;
      saveDiagnostics();
      pendingCommands[cmd.id] = { ws, ts: Date.now() };
      bridgeSocket.write(JSON.stringify(cmd) + "\n");
    } else if (msg.action === "ping") {
      ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: "pong" }));
    }
  }

  // --- TCP Server for bridge.jsx ---
  let bridgeSocket: net.Socket | null = null;
  let tcpBuffer = "";

  const tcpServer = net.createServer((socket) => {
    if (bridgeSocket && !bridgeSocket.destroyed) {
      bridgeSocket.destroy();
    }
    bridgeSocket = socket;
    tcpBuffer = "";
    
    // Log TCP handshake to telemetry metrics
    diagnostics.metrics.aeTcpConnectionsCount++;
    saveDiagnostics();
    
    console.log("[TCP] AE Bridge connected from", socket.remoteAddress);
    broadcastToBrowsers({ type: "bridge_status", connected: true });

    socket.on("data", (data) => {
      tcpBuffer += data.toString();
      const lines = tcpBuffer.split("\n");
      tcpBuffer = lines.pop() || "";
      for (const line of lines) {
        const trimmed = line.trim();
        if (!trimmed) continue;
        try {
          const msg = JSON.parse(trimmed);
          handleBridgeMessage(msg);
        } catch (e: any) {
          console.error("[TCP] Parse error:", e.message);
          logDiagnosticError("parse", "Unable to parse JSON from After Effects TCP stream", e.message);
        }
      }
    });

    socket.on("close", () => {
      console.log("[TCP] AE Bridge disconnected");
      bridgeSocket = null;
      broadcastToBrowsers({ type: "bridge_status", connected: false });
    });

    socket.on("error", (err) => {
      console.error("[TCP] Socket error:", err.message);
      logDiagnosticError("tcp", "After Effects TCP Socket error encountered", err.message);
    });
  });

  tcpServer.listen(TCP_PORT, "0.0.0.0", () => {
    console.log(`[TCP] TCP socket server listening on port ${TCP_PORT} (waiting for After Effects connection)`);
  });

  function handleBridgeMessage(msg: any) {
    if ((msg.type === "result" || msg.type === "error") && msg.id) {
      if (msg.type === "result") {
        diagnostics.metrics.commandsResolved++;
      } else {
        diagnostics.metrics.commandsFailed++;
        logDiagnosticError("ae_script", "After Effects ExtendScript error evaluation", msg.error);
      }
      saveDiagnostics();

      const pending = pendingCommands[msg.id];
      if (pending && pending.ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
        pending.ws.send(JSON.stringify(msg));
        delete pendingCommands[msg.id];
      }
    } else if (msg.type === "status") {
      broadcastToBrowsers(msg);
    }
  }

  // Clean stale commands
  setInterval(() => {
    const now = Date.now();
    for (const id in pendingCommands) {
      if (now - pendingCommands[id].ts > 15000) {
        const p = pendingCommands[id];
        diagnostics.metrics.commandsTimedOut++;
        logDiagnosticError("ae_script", "Command timed out waiting for After Effects response", "Incident Command Target Key: " + id);
        saveDiagnostics();
        
        if (p.ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
          p.ws.send(JSON.stringify({ 
            type: "error", 
            id, 
            error: "Command timed out waiting for After Effects" 
          }));
        }
        delete pendingCommands[id];
      }
    }
  }, 15000);


  // --- Vite Dev server integration ---
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production") {
    const vite = await createViteServer({
      server: { middlewareMode: true },
      appType: "spa",
    });
    app.use(vite.middlewares);
  } else {
    // Serve production static assets
    const distPath = path.join(process.cwd(), "dist");
    app.use(express.static(distPath));
    app.get("*", (req, res) => {
      res.sendFile(path.join(distPath, "index.html"));
    });
  }

  httpServer.listen(HTTP_PORT, "0.0.0.0", () => {
    console.log("==================================================");
    console.log(`  Touch Tools Full-Stack Server Active`);
    console.log(`  HTTP / WebSockets:  http://localhost:${HTTP_PORT}`);
    console.log(`  TCP Port for AE:    tcp://localhost:${TCP_PORT}`);
    console.log("==================================================");
  });
}

startServer().catch(err => {
  console.error("Failed to start Touch Tools server:", err);
});


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/App.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from "react";
import { Header } from "./components/Header";
import { CompSettingsPanel } from "./components/CompSettingsPanel";
import { Toolbar } from "./components/Toolbar";
import { TransportBar } from "./components/TransportBar";
import { InlineAccordions } from "./components/InlineAccordions";
import { ShapesPanel } from "./components/ShapesPanel";
import { CameraPanel } from "./components/CameraPanel";
import { TextPanel } from "./components/TextPanel";
import { XModePanel } from "./components/XModePanel";

import { Layer, CompSettings, CompItem } from "./types";
import { mockComps, getMockLayersForComp, getMockCompSettings } from "./mockData";
import { esc } from "./utils";
import { 
  ChevronDown, 
  Trash2, 
  Copy, 
  Scissors, 
  Eye, 
  Lock, 
  Unlock, 
  UserSquare2, 
  Globe, 
  ShieldAlert,
  Info
} from "lucide-react";

export default function App() {
  // System statuses
  const [wsConnected, setWsConnected] = useState(false);
  const [bridgeConnected, setBridgeConnected] = useState(false);
  const [isDemoMode, setIsDemoMode] = useState(false);

  // States
  const [compositions, setCompositions] = useState<CompItem[]>([]);
  const [selectedCompIndex, setSelectedCompIndex] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const [layers, setLayers] = useState<Layer[]>([]);
  const [selectedLayerIndex, setSelectedLayerIndex] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<"layers" | "shapes" | "camera" | "text" | "scripts">("layers");
  
  // Scrubber & Transport Settings
  const [currentTime, setCurrentTime] = useState(0.0);
  const [isPlaying, setIsPlaying] = useState(false);
  const [compSettings, setCompSettings] = useState<CompSettings>({
    width: 1920,
    height: 1080,
    frameRate: 30,
    duration: 15,
    bgColor: [0.03, 0.03, 0.04],
    motionBlur: true,
    name: "Main Intro Comp"
  });

  // UI States
  const [expandedLayerIndex, setExpandedLayerIndex] = useState<number | null>(null);
  const [compSettingsOpen, setCompSettingsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [toasts, setToasts] = useState<{ id: number; text: string; type: "success" | "error" | "info" }[]>([]);

  // WebSocket referencing
  const wsRef = useRef<WebSocket | null>(null);
  const cmdIdRef = useRef(0);
  const pendingCommandsRef = useRef<Map<string, { resolve: any; reject: any; timeout: any }>>(new Map());
  const inFlightUpdatesRef = useRef<Map<string, { params: any; isSending: boolean; nextParams: any | null; resolveNext: any }>>(new Map());

  // Toast notifier helper
  const triggerToast = (text: string, type: "success" | "error" | "info" = "success") => {
    const id = Date.now() + Math.random();
    setToasts(prev => [...prev, { id, text, type }]);
    setTimeout(() => {
      setToasts(prev => prev.filter(t => t.id !== id));
    }, 3000);
  };

  // --- WebSocket Connection Implementation ---
  useEffect(() => {
    const wsUrl = window.location.protocol === "https:" ? `wss://${window.location.host}` : `ws://${window.location.host}`;
    let socket: WebSocket;
    let reconInterval: any;

    function connect() {
      socket = new WebSocket(wsUrl);
      wsRef.current = socket;

      socket.onopen = () => {
        setWsConnected(true);
        triggerToast("Connected to Full-Stack server port 3000", "success");
      };

      socket.onclose = () => {
        setWsConnected(false);
        setBridgeConnected(false);
      };

      socket.onmessage = (ev) => {
        try {
          const msg = JSON.parse(ev.data);
          if (msg.type === "bridge_status") {
            setBridgeConnected(prev => {
              if (msg.connected && !prev) {
                setIsDemoMode(false); // disable demo mode immediately when AE bridge connects
                triggerToast("Adobe After Effects socket connection established!", "success");
                syncWithAfterEffects();
              } else if (!msg.connected && prev) {
                triggerToast("Adobe After Effects connection stepped down.", "info");
              }
              return msg.connected;
            });
          } else if (msg.type === "result" || msg.type === "error") {
            resolvePendingCommand(msg);
          }
        } catch (e) {
          console.error(e);
        }
      };
    }

    connect();

    reconInterval = setInterval(() => {
      if (wsRef.current?.readyState === WebSocket.CLOSED) {
        connect();
      }
    }, 5000);

    return () => {
      clearInterval(reconInterval);
      wsRef.current?.close();
    };
  }, []);

  // Sync data with Adobe After Effects
  const syncWithAfterEffects = async () => {
    const activeComp = await ae("getActiveComp");
    if (activeComp && !activeComp.error) {
      setSelectedCompIndex(activeComp.index);
      
      const compSet = await ae("getCompSettings", { compIndex: activeComp.index });
      if (compSet && !compSet.error) {
        setCompSettings({
          width: compSet.width,
          height: compSet.height,
          frameRate: compSet.frameRate,
          duration: compSet.duration,
          bgColor: compSet.bgColor || [0.03, 0.03, 0.04],
          motionBlur: !!compSet.motionBlur,
          name: compSet.name || activeComp.name
        });
      }

      await fetchLayersForComp(activeComp.index);
    }
  };

  const fetchLayersForComp = async (compIndex: number) => {
    const data = await ae("getLayers", { compIndex });
    if (data && data.layers) {
      setLayers(data.layers);
    }
  };

  // --- Send payload to AE ---
  const aeDirect = (action: string, params: any = {}): Promise<any> => {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      if (isDemoMode) {
        // Resolve immediately with default values for local simulation
        resolve({ success: true });
        return;
      }

      if (!wsRef.current || wsRef.current.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
        reject(new Error("Server socket not connected"));
        return;
      }

      const id = `${++cmdIdRef.current}_${Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 6)}`;
      const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
        pendingCommandsRef.current.delete(id);
        reject(new Error(`Action ${action} timed out`));
      }, 10000);

      pendingCommandsRef.current.set(id, { resolve, reject, timeout });
      wsRef.current.send(JSON.stringify({
        action: "sendToAE",
        command: { id, action, ...params }
      }));
    });
  };

  const ae = (action: string, params: any = {}): Promise<any> => {
    if (action !== "setValue") {
      return aeDirect(action, params);
    }

    const key = `${params.layerIndex}_${params.propertyPath}`;
    let inFlight = inFlightUpdatesRef.current.get(key);

    if (!inFlight) {
      inFlight = {
        params: params,
        isSending: false,
        nextParams: null,
        resolveNext: null
      };
      inFlightUpdatesRef.current.set(key, inFlight);
    }

    if (!inFlight.isSending) {
      inFlight.isSending = true;
      inFlight.params = params;
      const promise = aeDirect(action, params).finally(() => {
        inFlight!.isSending = false;
        if (inFlight!.nextParams) {
          const next = inFlight!.nextParams;
          const resolve = inFlight!.resolveNext;
          inFlight!.nextParams = null;
          inFlight!.resolveNext = null;
          ae(action, next).then(resolve);
        }
      });
      return promise;
    } else {
      inFlight.nextParams = params;
      if (inFlight.resolveNext) {
        inFlight.resolveNext({ success: true, superseded: true });
      }
      return new Promise((resolve) => {
        inFlight!.resolveNext = resolve;
      });
    }
  };

  const resolvePendingCommand = (msg: any) => {
    const p = pendingCommandsRef.current.get(msg.id);
    if (!p) return;
    clearTimeout(p.timeout);
    pendingCommandsRef.current.delete(msg.id);
    if (msg.type === "error" || msg.error) {
      p.reject(new Error(msg.error || "AE Error"));
    } else {
      p.resolve(msg.data);
    }
  };

  // --- Toggle Simulation offline support & loading datasets ---
  useEffect(() => {
    if (isDemoMode && selectedCompIndex) {
      setCompositions(mockComps);
      setLayers(getMockLayersForComp(selectedCompIndex));
      setCompSettings(getMockCompSettings(selectedCompIndex));
    } else if (!isDemoMode && wsConnected && bridgeConnected) {
      // Reload actual comp options
      ae("getComps").then(r => {
        if (r && r.comps) {
          setCompositions(r.comps);
        }
      });
    }
  }, [isDemoMode, selectedCompIndex, wsConnected, bridgeConnected]);

  // --- Scrubber Playback Simulation Frame Loop ---
  useEffect(() => {
    let animRef: any;
    if (isPlaying) {
      const fps = compSettings.frameRate;
      const intervalSec = 1 / fps;
      
      const loop = () => {
        setCurrentTime(prev => {
          const nextVal = prev + intervalSec;
          if (nextVal >= compSettings.duration) {
            return 0.0; // loop playback
          }
          return nextVal;
        });
        animRef = setTimeout(loop, intervalSec * 1000);
      };
      
      loop();
    } else {
      clearTimeout(animRef);
    }
    return () => clearTimeout(animRef);
  }, [isPlaying, compSettings]);

  // --- Active Tab Switching triggers ---
  const handleTabSwitch = (tab: "layers" | "shapes" | "camera" | "text" | "scripts") => {
    if (layers.length === 0) {
      triggerToast("No active composition layers. Select or Create layers.", "info");
    }
    setActiveTab(tab);
  };

  // --- Set parameter changes handlers ---
  const handleApplySettings = async (newSettings: CompSettings) => {
    setCompSettings(newSettings);
    triggerToast("Composition settings updated!", "success");
    if (!isDemoMode) {
      await ae("setCompSettings", {
        compIndex: selectedCompIndex,
        width: newSettings.width,
        height: newSettings.height,
        frameRate: newSettings.frameRate,
        duration: newSettings.duration,
        bgColor: newSettings.bgColor
      });
    }
  };

  const resetSettings = () => {
    if (isDemoMode) {
      setCompSettings(getMockCompSettings(selectedCompIndex || 1));
    } else {
      syncWithAfterEffects();
    }
    triggerToast("Settings reset to current configuration", "info");
  };

  const handleSelectComp = async (index: number) => {
    setSelectedCompIndex(index);
    if (!isDemoMode) {
      await ae("setActiveComp", { compIndex: index });
      await fetchLayersForComp(index);
    }
  };

  // --- Quick layer creation operators ---
  const handleCreateLayer = async (type: "solid" | "shape" | "text" | "null" | "camera" | "light", arg?: any) => {
    triggerToast(`Added ${type} layer`, "success");
    const newIdx = layers.length + 1;
    const newLayer: Layer = {
      index: newIdx,
      name: `${type.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + type.slice(1)} Controller`,
      enabled: true,
      locked: false,
      solo: false,
      shy: false,
      layerType: type,
      selected: false,
      parentIndex: null,
      stretch: 100
    };
    
    setLayers([...layers, newLayer]);

    if (!isDemoMode) {
      if (type === "solid") {
        await ae("createSolid", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, name: "Solid backdrop" });
      } else if (type === "text") {
        await ae("createText", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, text: "Touch Tools Title" });
      } else if (type === "null") {
        await ae("createNull", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, name: "Controller Null", threeD: true });
      } else if (type === "camera") {
        await ae("createCamera", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex });
      } else if (type === "light") {
        await ae("createLight", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex });
      } else if (type === "shape") {
        const shapeItem = await ae("createShape", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, name: `${arg || "Rectangle"} shape` });
        if (shapeItem && arg === "Rectangle") {
          await ae("addShapeRectangle", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, layerIndex: 1, name: "Rectangle", size: [200, 200] });
        } else if (shapeItem && arg === "Ellipse") {
          await ae("addShapeEllipse", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, layerIndex: 1, name: "Ellipse", size: [200, 200] });
        }
      }
      await fetchLayersForComp(selectedCompIndex || 1);
    }
  };

  const handleSelectLayerRow = (idx: number) => {
    setSelectedLayerIndex(idx);
    setLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.index === idx ? { ...l, selected: true } : { ...l, selected: false }));
    ae("selectLayer", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, layerIndex: idx });
  };

  // --- Inline Row Actions implementation ---
  const handleLayerUpdate = (idx: number, updatedProps: Partial<Layer>) => {
    setLayers(prev => prev.map(l => l.index === idx ? { ...l, ...updatedProps } : l));
  };

  const handleSplitLayer = async (idx: number) => {
    triggerToast("Split layer at current playhead frame", "success");
    if (!isDemoMode) {
      await ae("splitLayer", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, layerIndex: idx });
      await fetchLayersForComp(selectedCompIndex || 1);
    }
  };

  const handleDuplicateLayer = async (idx: number) => {
    triggerToast("Layer duplicated", "success");
    const target = layers.find(l => l.index === idx);
    if (target) {
      const dup: Layer = {
        ...target,
        index: layers.length + 1,
        name: `${target.name} Duplicate`
      };
      setLayers([...layers, dup]);
    }
    if (!isDemoMode) {
      await ae("duplicateLayer", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, layerIndex: idx });
      await fetchLayersForComp(selectedCompIndex || 1);
    }
  };

  const handleDeleteLayer = async (idx: number) => {
    triggerToast("Layer removed", "info");
    setLayers(layers.filter(l => l.index !== idx).map((l, i) => ({ ...l, index: i + 1 })));
    if (!isDemoMode) {
      await ae("deleteLayer", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, layerIndex: idx });
      await fetchLayersForComp(selectedCompIndex || 1);
    }
  };

  const handleLayerFlagToggle = async (idx: number, flag: "enabled" | "locked" | "solo" | "shy" | "motionBlur" | "adjustmentLayer" | "threeDLayer" | "collapseTransformations") => {
    const target = layers.find(l => l.index === idx);
    if (!target) return;
    const newVal = !target[flag];
    handleLayerUpdate(idx, { [flag]: newVal });
    triggerToast(`Toggled ${flag}`, "info");

    const flagESMap: any = {
      locked: "locked",
      solo: "solo",
      shy: "shy",
      motionBlur: "motionBlur",
      adjustmentLayer: "adjustmentLayer",
      enabled: "enabled",
      threeDLayer: "threeDLayer",
      collapseTransformations: "collapseTransformations"
    };

    if (!isDemoMode) {
      if (flag === "enabled") {
        await ae("setValue", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, layerIndex: idx, propertyPath: "enabled", value: newVal });
      } else {
        await ae("executeScript", {
          script: `try { app.project.activeItem.layer(${idx}).${flagESMap[flag]} = ${newVal}; } catch(err) { $.writeln("Skipped toggling: " + err.toString()); }`
        });
      }
    }
  };

  // --- Scrubber handlers ---
  const handleScrubTime = (newTime: number) => {
    setCurrentTime(newTime);
    if (!isDemoMode) {
      ae("setCurrentTime", { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, time: newTime });
    }
  };

  // --- Transport timeline buttons ---
  const handlePrevFrame = () => {
    const step = 1 / compSettings.frameRate;
    handleScrubTime(Math.max(0, currentTime - step));
  };

  const handleNextFrame = () => {
    const step = 1 / compSettings.frameRate;
    handleScrubTime(Math.min(compSettings.duration, currentTime + step));
  };

  const handlePrevKeyframe = () => {
    triggerToast("Go to previous keyframe", "info");
    ae("executeCommand", { commandId: 2429 });
  };

  const handleNextKeyframe = () => {
    triggerToast("Go to next keyframe", "info");
    ae("executeCommand", { commandId: 2430 });
  };

  // --- Speech voice command receiver / setter interpreter ---
  const handleExecuteVoiceCommand = (cmd: string) => {
    const c = cmd.toLowerCase().trim();
    if (c.startsWith("add solid")) {
      handleCreateLayer("solid");
    } else if (c.startsWith("add text")) {
      handleCreateLayer("text");
    } else if (c.startsWith("add null")) {
      handleCreateLayer("null");
    } else if (c.startsWith("add camera")) {
      handleCreateLayer("camera");
    } else if (c.startsWith("add light")) {
      handleCreateLayer("light");
    } else if (c === "zoom fit" || c === "fit") {
      triggerToast("Canvas fit executed", "info");
      ae("executeCommand", { commandId: 2003 });
    } else if (c === "grid" || c === "toggle grid") {
      triggerToast("Transparency grid toggled", "info");
      ae("executeCommand", { commandId: 3159 });
    } else if (c === "duplicate" && selectedLayerIndex) {
      handleDuplicateLayer(selectedLayerIndex);
    } else if (c === "delete" && selectedLayerIndex) {
      handleDeleteLayer(selectedLayerIndex);
    } else if (c === "split" && selectedLayerIndex) {
      handleSplitLayer(selectedLayerIndex);
    } else {
      triggerToast(`Raw execute: "${cmd}"`, "info");
      ae("executeScript", { script: cmd });
    }
  };

  // --- Undo/Redo commands ---
  const undo = () => {
    triggerToast("Undo executed", "info");
    ae("executeCommand", { commandId: 16 });
  };

  const redo = () => {
    triggerToast("Redo executed", "info");
    ae("executeCommand", { commandId: 17 });
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-screen bg-[#070709] text-white/90 overflow-hidden font-sans">
      {/* Toast Notification parade container */}
      <div className="fixed top-16 right-4 flex flex-col gap-2 z-[9999]">
        {toasts.map(t => (
          <div
            key={t.id}
            className={`px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-xs font-medium border shadow-2xl flex items-center gap-2 animate-fade-in transition-all-300 ${
              t.type === "success"
                ? "bg-[#10b981]/10 border-[#10b981]/30 text-emerald-300"
                : t.type === "error"
                ? "bg-rose-500/10 border-rose-500/30 text-rose-400"
                : "bg-amber-500/10 border-amber-500/30 text-amber-300"
            }`}
          >
            <Info className="w-3.5 h-3.5 flex-shrink-0" /> {t.text}
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Header element */}
      <Header
        bridgeConnected={bridgeConnected}
        wsConnected={wsConnected}
        compName={compSettings.name}
        onRenameComp={(newName) => {
          setCompSettings(prev => ({ ...prev, name: newName }));
          triggerToast("Composition renamed!", "success");
        }}
        onExecuteCommand={handleExecuteVoiceCommand}
        undo={undo}
        redo={redo}
      />

      {/* Configurator gear expansion layer settings */}
      <CompSettingsPanel
        settings={compSettings}
        onApplySettings={handleApplySettings}
        isOpen={compSettingsOpen}
        setIsOpen={setCompSettingsOpen}
        resetSettings={resetSettings}
      />

      {/* Custom dropdown toolbar */}
      <Toolbar
        compositions={compositions}
        selectedCompIndex={selectedCompIndex}
        onSelectComp={handleSelectComp}
        onRefresh={syncWithAfterEffects}
        onCanvasCommand={(cmd) => {
          const commandIDs = { zoomIn: 2016, zoomOut: 2017, fit: 2003, grid: 2573 };
          triggerToast(`Toggled canvas ${cmd}`, "info");
          ae("executeCommand", { commandId: commandIDs[cmd] });
        }}
        onCreateLayer={handleCreateLayer}
        compSettingsOpen={compSettingsOpen}
        onToggleCompSettings={() => setCompSettingsOpen(!compSettingsOpen)}
      />

      {/* Transport timeline scrubber panel */}
      <TransportBar
        isPlaying={isPlaying}
        onPlayToggle={() => setIsPlaying(!isPlaying)}
        currentTime={currentTime}
        duration={compSettings.duration}
        fps={compSettings.frameRate}
        onScrubTime={handleScrubTime}
        onPrevFrame={handlePrevFrame}
        onNextFrame={handleNextFrame}
        onPrevKeyframe={handlePrevKeyframe}
        onNextKeyframe={handleNextKeyframe}
        onGoStart={() => handleScrubTime(0.0)}
        onGoEnd={() => handleScrubTime(compSettings.duration)}
      />

      {/* Tab select strip buttons */}
      <nav className="tab-bar flex gap-1 px-6 py-2 border-b border-amber/20 bg-[#121217]/80 flex-shrink-0">
        {[
          { id: "layers", label: "Layers", icon: "▧" },
          { id: "shapes", label: "Shapes", icon: "◢" },
          { id: "camera", label: "Camera", icon: "📷" },
          { id: "text", label: "Text", icon: "T" },
          { id: "scripts", label: "X Mode", icon: ">_" }
        ].map(t => {
          const isActive = activeTab === t.id;
          return (
            <button
              key={t.id}
              onClick={() => handleTabSwitch(t.id as any)}
              className={`px-4 py-1 rounded-lg flex items-center gap-2 transition-all text-xs font-semibold select-none border ${
                isActive
                  ? "bg-[#e8a838]/15 text-[#e8a838] border-amber/40 shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(232,168,56,0.06)]"
                  : "text-white/40 hover:text-white/80 hover:bg-white/5 border-transparent"
              }`}
            >
              <span className={`font-mono text-xs ${isActive ? "text-[#e8a838]" : "text-white/30"}`}>{t.icon}</span>
              <span>{t.label}</span>
            </button>
          );
        })}
      </nav>

      {/* Main scrolling viewport views */}
      <main className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 md:p-6 bg-[#070709] font-sans">
        {activeTab === "layers" && (
          <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto flex flex-col gap-3">
            {layers.length === 0 ? (
              !bridgeConnected ? (
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-8 md:p-12 bg-[#121217]/60 border border-amber/20 rounded-2xl max-w-2xl mx-auto shadow-2xl animate-fade-in text-left">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-6">
                    <span className="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-rose-500/10 border border-rose-500/20 flex items-center justify-center text-rose-400 text-lg font-bold animate-pulse">!</span>
                    <div>
                      <h3 className="text-base font-bold text-white">After Effects Bridge Offline</h3>
                      <p className="text-xs text-white/40">Waiting for local ExtendScript socket connection</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  
                  <div className="space-y-4 text-xs text-white/70">
                    <p className="leading-relaxed border-b border-white/5 pb-3">
                      To enable real-time bidirectional controls and sync compositions, follow this simple setup with your latest After Effects version:
                    </p>
                    
                    <div className="flex gap-2.5">
                      <span className="font-mono text-[#e8a838] bg-[#e8a838]/10 w-5 h-5 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0 font-bold">1</span>
                      <p>
                        Enable network access in After Effects under <strong>Preferences &gt; Scripting &amp; Expressions</strong> &gt; check <strong>&quot;Allow Scripts to Write Files and Access Network&quot;</strong>.
                      </p>
                    </div>

                    <div className="flex gap-2.5">
                      <span className="font-mono text-[#e8a838] bg-[#e8a838]/10 w-5 h-5 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0 font-bold">2</span>
                      <p>
                        Execute the background script in After Effects: Choose <strong>File &gt; Scripts &gt; Run Script File...</strong> and browse to select <code>bridge.jsx</code> located in the workspace folder.
                      </p>
                    </div>

                    <div className="flex gap-2.5">
                      <span className="font-mono text-[#e8a838] bg-[#e8a838]/10 w-5 h-5 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center flex-shrink-0 font-bold">3</span>
                      <p>
                        The status indicator at the top left of this page will automatically light up <strong className="text-emerald-400">● CONNECTED TO AE</strong> and load your layers live!
                      </p>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  <div className="mt-8 pt-4 border-t border-white/5 flex flex-wrap gap-3 items-center justify-between w-full">
                    <span className="text-[10px] text-white/30 font-mono">Listening on Local Port: 8092</span>
                    <button 
                      onClick={syncWithAfterEffects}
                      className="px-4 py-2 bg-gradient-to-r from-amber-500 to-amber-600 hover:from-amber-600 hover:to-amber-700 text-black font-semibold text-xs rounded-xl shadow-lg transition-all"
                    >
                      🔄 Re-Sync Now
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-center p-20 bg-[#121217]/50 border border-amber/15 rounded-2xl">
                  <span className="text-4xl mb-3 opacity-30 text-[#e8a838]">📁</span>
                  <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-white/90">No layers in this composition</h3>
                  <p className="text-xs text-white/40 max-w-sm mt-1 mb-4">
                    Create solids, shapes, or texts using the creator buttons on the toolbar to add elements automatically in AE.
                  </p>
                </div>
              )
            ) : (
              layers.map((l) => {
                const isSelected = selectedLayerIndex === l.index;
                const isExpanded = expandedLayerIndex === l.index;
                
                return (
                  <div
                    key={l.index}
                    className={`layer-container border transition-all duration-200 rounded-xl overflow-hidden ${
                      isSelected
                        ? "border-[#e8a838] bg-[#121217] shadow-[0_4px_30px_rgba(0,0,0,0.5)]"
                        : "border-amber/10 bg-[#121217]/60 hover:bg-[#121217]"
                    }`}
                  >
                    {/* Main Row */}
                    <div
                      className="layer-item-row flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between p-3.5 gap-3 cursor-pointer user-select-none"
                      onClick={() => handleSelectLayerRow(l.index)}
                    >
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2.5">
                        {/* Expand drawer accordion chevron toggler */}
                        <button
                          onClick={(e) => {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            setExpandedLayerIndex(isExpanded ? null : l.index);
                          }}
                          className={`w-6 h-6 rounded bg-white/5 border border-white/5 flex items-center justify-center hover:bg-white/10 transition-colors text-white/60 ${
                            isExpanded ? "text-[#e8a838]" : ""
                          }`}
                        >
                          <ChevronDown className={`w-3.5 h-3.5 transition-transform duration-200 ${isExpanded ? "transform rotate-180" : ""}`} />
                        </button>

                        <span className="font-mono text-[10px] text-white/30 tracking-tight">{l.index}</span>

                        {/* Visibility and Locks Flags status button */}
                        <button
                          onClick={(e) => {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            handleLayerFlagToggle(l.index, "enabled");
                          }}
                          className={`text-xs pl-1 ${l.enabled ? "opacity-100" : "opacity-30"}`}
                          title="Toggle Visibility"
                        >
                          {l.enabled ? "👁️" : "🕶️"}
                        </button>

                        <button
                          onClick={(e) => {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            handleLayerFlagToggle(l.index, "locked");
                          }}
                          className={`text-xs px-0.5 ${l.locked ? "text-[#e8a838] opacity-100 font-bold" : "opacity-30"}`}
                          title="Toggle Lock"
                        >
                          {l.locked ? <Lock className="w-3 h-3 text-[#e8a838]" /> : <Unlock className="w-3 h-3" />}
                        </button>

                        <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-white/95 tracking-wide max-w-[200px] truncate">
                          {l.name}
                        </span>

                        <span className="text-[9px] font-mono tracking-widest uppercase text-white/40 bg-[#070709] px-2 py-0.5 rounded border border-white/5">
                          {l.layerType}
                        </span>
                      </div>

                      {/* Right actions trigger buttons */}
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 self-end sm:self-auto bg-black/40 p-1 rounded-lg border border-white/5 shrink-0">
                        {/* Quick controls faders */}
                        <button
                          onClick={(e) => {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            handleSplitLayer(l.index);
                          }}
                          className="p-1 px-2 hover:bg-white/5 text-white/40 hover:text-white/80 rounded transition-all text-[10px] uppercase font-bold flex items-center gap-1"
                          title="Split Layer"
                        >
                          <Scissors className="w-3 h-3" /> Split
                        </button>
                        <button
                          onClick={(e) => {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            handleDuplicateLayer(l.index);
                          }}
                          className="p-1 px-2 hover:bg-white/5 text-white/40 hover:text-white/80 rounded transition-all text-[10px] uppercase font-bold flex items-center gap-1"
                          title="Duplicate"
                        >
                          <Copy className="w-3 h-3" /> Duplicate
                        </button>
                        <button
                          onClick={(e) => {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            handleDeleteLayer(l.index);
                          }}
                          className="p-1 px-2 hover:bg-rose-500/10 text-rose-400/60 hover:text-rose-400 rounded transition-all text-[10px] uppercase font-bold flex items-center gap-1"
                          title="Remove Layer"
                        >
                          <Trash2 className="w-3 h-3" /> Delete
                        </button>
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    {/* Collapsible expanded drawer system accordion wrapper */}
                    {isExpanded && (
                      <div className="bg-[#070709]/80 border-t border-white/[0.04] p-4 font-sans max-h-[1500px]">
                        {/* Flag Chips checklist */}
                        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5 mb-3.5">
                          {[
                            { flag: "solo" as const, label: "Solo" },
                            { flag: "shy" as const, label: "Shy" },
                            { flag: "motionBlur" as const, label: "Motion Blur" },
                            { flag: "adjustmentLayer" as const, label: "Adjustment" },
                            { flag: "threeDLayer" as const, label: "3D Layer" },
                            { flag: "collapseTransformations" as const, label: "Cont. Rasterize" }
                          ].map(item => (
                            <button
                              key={item.flag}
                              onClick={() => handleLayerFlagToggle(l.index, item.flag)}
                              className={`px-2 py-1 text-[9px] font-bold uppercase rounded border transition-all ${
                                l[item.flag]
                                  ? "bg-[#e8a838]/15 border-[#e8a838] text-[#e8a838] shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(232,168,56,0.1)]"
                                  : "border-white/5 text-white/40 hover:border-white/10 hover:text-white"
                              }`}
                            >
                              {item.label}
                            </button>
                          ))}
                        </div>

                        {/* Inline Expand Accordions Drawer */}
                        <InlineAccordions
                          layer={l}
                          isDemoMode={isDemoMode}
                          ae={ae}
                          onLayerUpdate={(vals) => handleLayerUpdate(l.index, vals)}
                          layersList={layers}
                        />
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                );
              })
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 2. Custom Shapes Panel */}
        {activeTab === "shapes" && (
          <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
            <ShapesPanel
              layerList={layers}
              selectedLayerIndex={selectedLayerIndex}
              onSelectLayer={handleSelectLayerRow}
              onAddShape={async (stype) => {
                triggerToast(`Added Shape vector element ${stype}`, "success");
                if (!isDemoMode && selectedLayerIndex) {
                  const cmdMap: any = {
                    Rectangle: "addShapeRectangle",
                    Ellipse: "addShapeEllipse"
                  };
                  await ae(cmdMap[stype], { compIndex: selectedCompIndex, layerIndex: selectedLayerIndex, name: stype, size: [200, 200] });
                }
              }}
            />
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 3. Custom Camera Options View */}
        {activeTab === "camera" && (
          <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
            <CameraPanel
              layerList={layers}
              selectedLayerIndex={selectedLayerIndex}
              onSelectLayer={handleSelectLayerRow}
              isDemoMode={isDemoMode}
              ae={ae}
            />
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 4. Text Modification Document panel */}
        {activeTab === "text" && (
          <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
            <TextPanel
              layerList={layers}
              selectedLayerIndex={selectedLayerIndex}
              onSelectLayer={handleSelectLayerRow}
              isDemoMode={isDemoMode}
              ae={ae}
            />
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 5. Terminal execution console */}
        {activeTab === "scripts" && (
          <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto h-full flex flex-col justify-between">
            <XModePanel isDemoMode={isDemoMode} ae={ae} />
          </div>
        )}
      </main>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: src/components/CameraPanel.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState } from "react";
import { Layer } from "../types";
import { Sliders } from "lucide-react";

interface CameraPanelProps {
  layerList: Layer[];
  selectedLayerIndex: number | null;
  onSelectLayer: (idx: number) => void;
  isDemoMode: boolean;
  ae: (action: string, params?: any) => Promise<any>;
}

export const CameraPanel: React.FC<CameraPanelProps> = ({
  layerList,
  selectedLayerIndex,
  onSelectLayer,
  isDemoMode,
  ae
}) => {
  const cameraLayers = layerList.filter(l => l.layerType === "camera");

  const [aperture, setAperture] = useState(50);
  const [focalLength, setFocalLength] = useState(50);
  const [focusDistance, setFocusDistance] = useState(1000);

  const applyCameraChange = (prop: string, v: number) => {
    if (!isDemoMode && selectedLayerIndex) {
      ae("setValue", {
        compIndex: null,
        layerIndex: selectedLayerIndex,
        propertyPath: `ADBE Camera Options Group/${prop}`,
        value: v
      });
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 bg-[#121217] border border-white/5 p-4 rounded-xl">
        <span className="text-xs text-white/50 font-sans font-bold uppercase">Focus Target</span>
        <select
          value={selectedLayerIndex || ""}
          onChange={(e) => onSelectLayer(parseInt(e.target.value) || 0)}
          className="sel bg-[#070709] border border-white/5 text-white text-xs px-2.5 py-1.5 rounded-lg outline-none cursor-pointer min-w-[200px]"
        >
          <option value="">Select Camera...</option>
          {cameraLayers.map(l => (
            <option key={l.index} value={l.index}>
              {l.index}. {l.name}
            </option>
          ))}
        </select>
      </div>

      <div className="bg-[#121217] border border-white/5 p-5 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4">
        <h3 className="text-xs font-bold tracking-wider text-[#e8a838] font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1.5">
          <Layers className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Camera Parameters Options
        </h3>

        <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 max-w-lg">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-white/40 w-24 uppercase">Aperture</span>
            <input
              type="range"
              min="0"
              max="200"
              value={aperture}
              onChange={(e) => {
                const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                setAperture(v);
                applyCameraChange("ADBE Camera Aperture", v);
              }}
              className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
            />
            <span className="w-12 font-mono text-xs text-right text-white/80">{aperture} mm</span>
          </div>

          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-white/40 w-24 uppercase">Focal Length</span>
            <input
              type="range"
              min="15"
              max="200"
              value={focalLength}
              onChange={(e) => {
                const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                setFocalLength(v);
                applyCameraChange("ADBE Camera Focal Length", v);
              }}
              className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
            />
            <span className="w-12 font-mono text-xs text-right text-white/80">{focalLength} mm</span>
          </div>

          <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
            <span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-white/40 w-24 uppercase">Focus Dist</span>
            <input
              type="range"
              min="100"
              max="5000"
              value={focusDistance}
              onChange={(e) => {
                const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                setFocusDistance(v);
                applyCameraChange("ADBE Camera Focus Distance", v);
              }}
              className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
            />
            <span className="w-12 font-mono text-xs text-right text-white/80">{focusDistance} px</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

FILE: src/components/CompSettingsPanel.tsx
