import React, { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import { CompSettings } from "../types";
import { rgbToHex, hexToRgb } from "../utils";
import { Settings, Check, RefreshCw } from "lucide-react";

interface CompSettingsPanelProps {
  settings: CompSettings;
  onApplySettings: (settings: CompSettings) => void;
  isOpen: boolean;
  setIsOpen: (val: boolean) => void;
  resetSettings: () => void;
}

export const CompSettingsPanel: React.FC<CompSettingsPanelProps> = ({
  settings,
  onApplySettings,
  isOpen,
  setIsOpen,
  resetSettings
}) => {
  const [width, setWidth] = useState(settings.width);
  const [height, setHeight] = useState(settings.height);
  const [frameRate, setFrameRate] = useState(settings.frameRate);
  const [duration, setDuration] = useState(settings.duration);
  const [hexColor, setHexColor] = useState("#000000");
  const [motionBlur, setMotionBlur] = useState(settings.motionBlur);
  const [hideShyLayers, setHideShyLayers] = useState(settings.hideShyLayers || false);

  useEffect(() => {
    setWidth(settings.width);
    setHeight(settings.height);
    setFrameRate(settings.frameRate);
    setDuration(settings.duration);
    setMotionBlur(settings.motionBlur);
    setHideShyLayers(settings.hideShyLayers || false);
    
    const r = Math.round(settings.bgColor[0] * 255);
    const g = Math.round(settings.bgColor[1] * 255);
    const b = Math.round(settings.bgColor[2] * 255);
    setHexColor(rgbToHex(r, g, b));
  }, [settings]);

  const applyPreset = (w: number, h: number) => {
    setWidth(w);
    setHeight(h);
  };

  const handleApply = () => {
    const rgb = hexToRgb(hexColor);
    onApplySettings({
      width,
      height,
      frameRate,
      duration,
      bgColor: [rgb.r / 255, rgb.g / 255, rgb.b / 255],
      motionBlur,
      hideShyLayers,
      name: settings.name
    });
    setIsOpen(false);
  };

  const selectColorPreset = (hex: string) => {
    setHexColor(hex);
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={`bg-[#121217]/95 backdrop-blur-xl border-b border-white/5 transition-all duration-300 ease-in-out overflow-hidden flex-shrink-0 ${
        isOpen ? "max-h-[500px] py-4 px-6 border-b" : "max-h-0"
      }`}
    >
      <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto flex flex-col gap-4">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-white/5 pb-2">
          <h3 className="text-xs font-bold tracking-wider text-[#e8a838] font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1.5">
            <Settings className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Composition Settings Parameters
          </h3>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <button
              onClick={resetSettings}
              className="px-2.5 py-1 text-[10px] text-white/60 hover:text-white border border-white/10 hover:border-white/20 rounded font-sans transition-all flex items-center gap-1"
            >
              <RefreshCw className="w-2.5 h-2.5" /> Reset
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={handleApply}
              className="px-3 py-1 bg-[#e8a838] text-[#070709] text-[10px] font-bold rounded hover:bg-[#e8a838]/90 transition-all font-sans"
            >
              Apply Settings
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6 text-white/80">
          {/* Left Column */}
          <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
            {/* Resolution */}
            <div className="flex items-start lg:items-center flex-col lg:flex-row gap-2">
              <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-white/40 font-sans uppercase w-20">Resolution</span>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                <input
                  type="number"
                  value={width}
                  onChange={(e) => setWidth(parseInt(e.target.value) || 0)}
                  className="w-16 bg-[#0f0f12] border border-white/5 text-white text-xs text-center py-1 rounded font-mono"
                  placeholder="W"
                />
                <span className="text-white/30 text-xs">×</span>
                <input
                  type="number"
                  value={height}
                  onChange={(e) => setHeight(parseInt(e.target.value) || 0)}
                  className="w-16 bg-[#0f0f12] border border-white/5 text-white text-xs text-center py-1 rounded font-mono"
                  placeholder="H"
                />
                
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
                  <button onClick={() => applyPreset(1920, 1080)} className="px-2 py-0.5 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-[10px] font-medium rounded text-white/70 transition-all">16:9</button>
                  <button onClick={() => applyPreset(1080, 1920)} className="px-2 py-0.5 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-[10px] font-medium rounded text-white/70 transition-all">9:16</button>
                  <button onClick={() => applyPreset(1080, 1080)} className="px-2 py-0.5 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-[10px] font-medium rounded text-white/70 transition-all">1:1</button>
                  <button onClick={() => applyPreset(2560, 1440)} className="px-2 py-0.5 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-[10px] font-medium rounded text-white/70 transition-all">2K</button>
                  <button onClick={() => applyPreset(3840, 2160)} className="px-2 py-0.5 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-[10px] font-medium rounded text-white/70 transition-all">4K</button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Framerate */}
            <div className="flex items-start lg:items-center flex-col lg:flex-row gap-2">
              <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-white/40 font-sans uppercase w-20">Frame Rate</span>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                {[23.976, 24, 29.97, 30, 60].map((fps) => (
                  <button
                    key={fps}
                    onClick={() => setFrameRate(fps)}
                    className={`px-2 py-1 text-[10px] font-medium rounded border transition-all ${
                      frameRate === fps
                        ? "bg-[#e8a838]/15 border-[#e8a838] text-[#e8a838]"
                        : "bg-[#070709] border-white/5 text-white/60 hover:border-white/10 hover:text-white"
                    }`}
                  >
                    {fps}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Duration */}
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-white/40 font-sans uppercase w-20">Duration</span>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <input
                  type="number"
                  value={duration}
                  step="0.1"
                  onChange={(e) => setDuration(parseFloat(e.target.value) || 0)}
                  className="w-20 bg-[#0f0f12] border border-white/5 text-white text-xs py-1 px-2 rounded font-mono text-left"
                />
                <span className="text-white/40 text-xs">seconds</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Right Column */}
          <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
            {/* Background Color */}
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-white/40 font-sans uppercase w-28">Background</span>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <div
                  className="w-6 h-6 rounded-md border border-white/15 cursor-pointer flex-shrink-0"
                  style={{ backgroundColor: hexColor }}
                  onClick={() => document.getElementById("csNativeColor")?.click()}
                />
                <input
                  type="color"
                  id="csNativeColor"
                  value={hexColor}
                  onChange={(e) => setHexColor(e.target.value)}
                  className="hidden"
                />
                <span className="text-xs text-white/60 font-mono tracking-wider">{hexColor.toUpperCase()}</span>

                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 ml-2">
                  {["#000000", "#121217", "#ff0000", "#00ff00", "#0000ff"].map((c) => (
                    <button
                      key={c}
                      onClick={() => selectColorPreset(c)}
                      className="w-3.5 h-3.5 rounded-full border border-white/10 hover:scale-110 transition-transform"
                      style={{ backgroundColor: c }}
                      title={c}
                    />
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Toggles */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 pt-1">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-white/40 font-sans uppercase">Motion Blur</span>
                <button
                  onClick={() => setMotionBlur(!motionBlur)}
                  className={`w-9 h-5 rounded-full relative transition-colors ${
                    motionBlur ? "bg-[#e8a838]" : "bg-white/10"
                  }`}
                >
                  <span
                    className={`absolute top-0.5 left-0.5 w-4 h-4 rounded-full bg-white shadow transition-transform ${
                      motionBlur ? "transform translateX(16px)" : ""
                    }`}
                  />
                </button>
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-white/40 font-sans uppercase">Hide Shy Layers</span>
                <button
                  onClick={() => setHideShyLayers(!hideShyLayers)}
                  className={`w-9 h-5 rounded-full relative transition-colors ${
                    hideShyLayers ? "bg-[#e8a838]" : "bg-white/10"
                  }`}
                >
                  <span
                    className={`absolute top-0.5 left-0.5 w-4 h-4 rounded-full bg-white shadow transition-transform ${
                      hideShyLayers ? "transform translateX(16px)" : ""
                    }`}
                  />
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/Header.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import { Mic, Check, Play, CornerDownLeft, Eye, Edit2, AlertCircle, Undo, Redo } from "lucide-react";

interface HeaderProps {
  bridgeConnected: boolean;
  wsConnected: boolean;
  compName: string;
  onRenameComp: (newName: string) => void;
  onExecuteCommand: (cmd: string) => void;
  undo: () => void;
  redo: () => void;
}

export const Header: React.FC<HeaderProps> = ({
  bridgeConnected,
  wsConnected,
  compName,
  onRenameComp,
  onExecuteCommand,
  undo,
  redo
}) => {
  const [isEditingName, setIsEditingName] = useState(false);
  const [editedName, setEditedName] = useState(compName);
  const [setterText, setSetterText] = useState("");
  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    setEditedName(compName);
  }, [compName]);

  const handleStartEdit = () => {
    setIsEditingName(true);
    setEditedName(compName);
  };

  const handleSaveEdit = () => {
    if (editedName.trim() && editedName.trim() !== compName) {
      onRenameComp(editedName.trim());
    }
    setIsEditingName(false);
  };

  const handleSetterRun = () => {
    if (setterText.trim()) {
      onExecuteCommand(setterText.trim());
      setSetterText("");
    }
  };

  const startListening = () => {
    const SpeechRecognition = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;
    if (!SpeechRecognition) {
      alert("Web Speech API is not supported in this browser. Please type the command in the Setter bar.");
      return;
    }

    const rec = new SpeechRecognition();
    rec.continuous = false;
    rec.interimResults = false;
    rec.lang = "en-US";

    rec.onstart = () => {
      setIsListening(true);
    };

    rec.onerror = (e: any) => {
      console.error(e);
      setIsListening(false);
    };

    rec.onend = () => {
      setIsListening(false);
    };

    rec.onresult = (e: any) => {
      const resultText = e.results[0][0].transcript;
      setSetterText(resultText);
      // auto execute after short delay
      setTimeout(() => {
        onExecuteCommand(resultText);
        setSetterText("");
      }, 700);
    };

    rec.start();
  };

  const getStatusColorClass = () => {
    if (bridgeConnected) return "bg-green-500 shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(34,197,94,0.6)]";
    if (wsConnected) return "bg-amber-500 shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(245,158,11,0.6)] animate-pulse";
    return "bg-rose-500 shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(244,63,94,0.6)] animate-pulse";
  };

  const getStatusText = () => {
    if (bridgeConnected) return "CONNECTED TO AE";
    if (wsConnected) return "SERVER ACTIVE (WAITING FOR AE)";
    return "SERVER DISCONNECTED";
  };

  return (
    <header className="header flex items-center justify-between px-6 bg-[#121217]/60 backdrop-blur-md border-b border-amber/20 h-12 flex-shrink-0 z-[100] gap-4">
      {/* Left side */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <h1 className="text-sm font-bold tracking-tight font-sans text-white">
          Touch<span className="text-[#e8a838]">Tools</span>
        </h1>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${getStatusColorClass()}`} />
          <span className="text-[10px] font-semibold text-white/40 tracking-wider font-mono uppercase hidden sm:inline">
            {getStatusText()}
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Center Side */}
      <div className="flex-1 max-w-xl mx-auto flex items-center gap-3 justify-center">
        {/* Composition Title Rename */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          {isEditingName ? (
            <input
              type="text"
              value={editedName}
              onChange={(e) => setEditedName(e.target.value)}
              onBlur={handleSaveEdit}
              onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === "Enter" && handleSaveEdit()}
              autoFocus
              className="bg-[#0f0f12] border border-[#e8a838] text-white text-[11px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded outline-none w-36 font-sans font-medium"
            />
          ) : (
            <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 cursor-pointer max-w-[150px] md:max-w-[200px]" onClick={handleStartEdit}>
              <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-white/90 truncate">
                {compName || "No active composition"}
              </span>
              <Edit2 className="w-2.5 h-2.5 text-white/40 hover:text-white transition-colors flex-shrink-0" />
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Natural Language Setter Bar */}
        <div className="flex-1 flex items-center bg-[#070709] border border-amber/15 rounded px-2 py-0.5 focus-within:border-[#e8a838]/60 focus-within:shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(232,168,56,0.15)] transition-all-300">
          <input
            type="text"
            value={setterText}
            onChange={(e) => setSetterText(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === "Enter" && handleSetterRun()}
            placeholder="add shape rect, rename to Title, zoom fit..."
            className="bg-transparent border-none text-white text-xs outline-none flex-1 min-width-0 px-2 font-sans placeholder-white/30"
          />
          <button
            onClick={startListening}
            className={`p-1 rounded text-white/50 hover:text-white transition-all flex-shrink-0 ${
              isListening ? "text-[#e8a838] bg-[#e8a838]/10 animate-mic-pulse" : "hover:bg-white/5"
            }`}
            title="Speech Voice Command"
          >
            <Mic className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={handleSetterRun}
            className="ml-1 px-2.5 py-0.5 bg-[#e8a838] text-[#070709] text-[10px] font-bold rounded hover:bg-[#e8a838]/80 transition-all font-sans uppercase"
          >
            RUN
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Right side - Undo/Redo */}
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
        <button
          onClick={undo}
          className="p-1 px-2 rounded-lg border border-white/5 bg-[#121217] text-white/60 hover:text-white hover:bg-white/5 transition-all text-[10px] flex items-center gap-1 font-bold uppercase tracking-wide cursor-pointer"
          title="Undo Action"
        >
          <Undo className="w-3 h-3 text-amber-500" /> Undo
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={redo}
          className="p-1 px-2 rounded-lg border border-white/5 bg-[#121217] text-white/60 hover:text-white hover:bg-white/5 transition-all text-[10px] flex items-center gap-1 font-bold uppercase tracking-wide cursor-pointer"
          title="Redo Action"
        >
          Redo <Redo className="w-3 h-3 text-amber-500" />
        </button>
      </div>
    </header>
  );
};


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/InlineAccordions.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef } from "react";
import { Layer, Effect, Mask, Keyframe } from "../types";
import { rgbToHex, hexToRgb } from "../utils";
import { Search, Plus, Trash2, Shield, Eye, Volume2, Move, Minimize, Sliders, Type, Scissors, Copy, Layers, Key } from "lucide-react";

interface InlineAccordionsProps {
  layer: Layer;
  isDemoMode: boolean;
  ae: (action: string, params?: any) => Promise<any>;
  onLayerUpdate: (updated: Partial<Layer>) => void;
  layersList: Layer[]; // for parent selection dropdown
}

export const InlineAccordions: React.FC<InlineAccordionsProps> = ({
  layer,
  isDemoMode,
  ae,
  onLayerUpdate,
  layersList
}) => {
  const [activeAcc, setActiveAcc] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // --- Local states for parameters (simulated locally for crisp feel) ---
  const [parentIndex, setParentIndex] = useState(layer.parentIndex || 0);
  const [blendMode, setBlendMode] = useState(layer.blendMode || "Normal");
  const [stretch, setStretch] = useState(layer.stretch || 100);

  // Transform parameters
  const [posX, setPosX] = useState(layer.layerType === "camera" ? 960 : 540);
  const [posY, setPosY] = useState(layer.layerType === "camera" ? 540 : 540);
  const [scaleX, setScaleX] = useState(100);
  const [scaleY, setScaleY] = useState(100);
  const [rotation, setRotation] = useState(0);
  const [opacity, setOpacity] = useState(100);

  // Audio decibels
  const [audioDb, setAudioDb] = useState(0.0);

  // Styling & effects parameters
  const [fillColor, setFillColor] = useState("#e8a838");
  const [strokeColor, setStrokeColor] = useState("#ffffff");
  const [strokeWidth, setStrokeWidth] = useState(2);
  const [shadowOpacity, setShadowOpacity] = useState(128);
  const [shadowDistance, setShadowDistance] = useState(10);
  const [shadowSoftness, setShadowSoftness] = useState(15);

  // Trackpad specific states
  const [trackpadMode, setTrackpadMode] = useState<"position" | "scale" | "rotation" | "anchor">("position");
  const [isAltPressed, setIsAltPressed] = useState(false);
  const [isShiftPressed, setIsShiftPressed] = useState(false);
  const trackpadRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  // Effects states
  const [fxQuery, setFxQuery] = useState("");
  const [fxList, setFxList] = useState<Effect[]>([
    { index: 1, name: "Gaussian Blur", matchName: "ADBE Gaussian Blur 2" }
  ]);
  const [glowIntensity, setGlowIntensity] = useState(1.0);

  // Masks
  const [masks, setMasks] = useState<Mask[]>([]);

  // Keyframes
  const [kfPropPath, setKfPropPath] = useState("");
  const [keyframes, setKeyframes] = useState<Keyframe[]>([]);

  // Sync state initially
  useEffect(() => {
    setParentIndex(layer.parentIndex || 0);
    setBlendMode(layer.blendMode || "Normal");
    setStretch(layer.stretch || 100);
    
    if (isDemoMode) {
      if (layer.layerType === "shape") {
        setPosX(250); setPosY(250);
      } else if (layer.layerType === "text") {
        setPosX(960); setPosY(540);
      }
    } else {
      // Fetch initial details when accordion expands
      if (activeAcc === "transform") {
        fetchAEProperties();
      } else if (activeAcc === "styling") {
        fetchAEStyling();
      } else if (activeAcc === "masks") {
        fetchAEMasks();
      }
    }
  }, [layer, activeAcc]);

  const fetchAEProperties = async () => {
    const data = await ae("getLayerProperties", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index });
    if (data && data.properties) {
      const tfGroup = data.properties.find((p: any) => p.matchName === "ADBE Transform Group");
      if (tfGroup && tfGroup.properties) {
        const getV = (mName: string) => tfGroup.properties.find((p: any) => p.matchName === mName)?.value;
        const pos = getV("ADBE Position");
        if (pos && Array.isArray(pos)) {
          setPosX(pos[0]); setPosY(pos[1]);
        }
        const scl = getV("ADBE Scale");
        if (scl && Array.isArray(scl)) {
          setScaleX(scl[0]); setScaleY(scl[1]);
        }
        const rot = getV("ADBE Rotate Z") ?? getV("ADBE Rotation");
        if (rot !== undefined) setRotation(rot);
        
        const opc = getV("ADBE Opacity");
        if (opc !== undefined) setOpacity(opc);
      }
    }
  };

  const fetchAEStyling = async () => {
    // Volume level query
    const audioRes = await ae("getProperty", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, propertyPath: "ADBE Audio Group/ADBE Audio Levels" });
    if (audioRes && audioRes.value !== undefined) {
      const levels = audioRes.value;
      setAudioDb(Array.isArray(levels) ? levels[0] : (levels || 0.0));
    }
  };

  const fetchAEMasks = async () => {
    const data = await ae("getMasks", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index });
    if (data && data.masks) {
      setMasks(data.masks);
    }
  };

  const toggleAccordion = (name: string) => {
    setActiveAcc(activeAcc === name ? null : name);
  };

  const handleParentChange = (val: number) => {
    setParentIndex(val);
    ae("setParent", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, parentIndex: val });
    onLayerUpdate({ parentIndex: val });
  };

  const handleBlendChange = (val: string) => {
    setBlendMode(val);
    ae("setBlendMode", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, mode: val });
    onLayerUpdate({ blendMode: val });
  };

  const handleStretchChange = (val: number) => {
    setStretch(val);
    ae("setTimeStretch", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, stretch: val });
    onLayerUpdate({ stretch: val });
  };

  const handleReverseToggle = () => {
    const newStretch = stretch * -1;
    setStretch(newStretch);
    ae("reverseLayer", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index });
    onLayerUpdate({ stretch: newStretch });
  };

  // --- Realtime slider updates with AE connection ---
  const applyParamChange = (path: string, val: any) => {
    if (!isDemoMode) {
      ae("setValue", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, propertyPath: path, value: val });
    }
  };

  // --- Visual Trackpad drag controller ---
  const handleTrackpadPointer = (e: React.PointerEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    if (!trackpadRef.current) return;
    setIsAltPressed(e.altKey);
    setIsShiftPressed(e.shiftKey);
    
    const rect = trackpadRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
    const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
    
    // Normalize coordinates -50 to +50 delta percent increments
    const dx = (x / rect.width) * 100 - 50;
    const dy = (y / rect.height) * 100 - 50;

    const mult = e.altKey ? 0.1 : e.shiftKey ? 10 : 1;

    if (trackpadMode === "position") {
      const nx = posX + dx * mult;
      const ny = posY + dy * mult;
      setPosX(Math.round(nx));
      setPosY(Math.round(ny));
      applyParamChange("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Position", [nx, ny]);
    } else if (trackpadMode === "scale") {
      const nsx = Math.max(0, scaleX + dx * mult * 0.5);
      const nsy = Math.max(0, scaleY + dy * mult * 0.5);
      setScaleX(Math.round(nsx));
      setScaleY(Math.round(nsy));
      applyParamChange("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Scale", [nsx, nsy]);
    } else if (trackpadMode === "rotation") {
      const nrot = rotation + dx * mult * 0.4;
      setRotation(Math.round(nrot));
      applyParamChange("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Rotate Z", nrot);
    }
  };

  const setParamKeyframe = (path: string) => {
    ae("setKeyframe", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, propertyPath: path });
    alert(`Keyframe created on ${path}`);
  };

  // --- Audio levels decibels adjuster ---
  const handleVolumeChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
    const val = parseFloat(e.target.value);
    setAudioDb(val);
    applyParamChange("ADBE Audio Group/ADBE Audio Levels", [val, val]);
  };

  // --- Effects searchable lists ---
  const effectsPresets = [
    { name: "Gaussian Blur", matchName: "ADBE Gaussian Blur 2" },
    { name: "Brightness & Contrast", matchName: "ADBE Brightness & Contrast 2" },
    { name: "Glow", matchName: "ADBE Glow 2" },
    { name: "Tint", matchName: "ADBE Tint" },
    { name: "Drop Shadow", matchName: "ADBE Drop Shadow" }
  ];

  const handleAddEffect = (matchName: string, name: string) => {
    const newFx: Effect = { index: fxList.length + 1, name, matchName };
    setFxList([...fxList, newFx]);
    ae("addEffect", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, effectMatchName: matchName });
    setFxQuery("");
  };

  const handleRemoveEffect = (fxIndex: number) => {
    setFxList(fxList.filter(f => f.index !== fxIndex));
    ae("removeEffect", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, effectIndex: fxIndex });
  };

  // --- Masks triggers ---
  const handleAddMask = () => {
    const newIndex = masks.length + 1;
    const newMask: Mask = {
      index: newIndex,
      name: `Mask ${newIndex}`,
      maskMode: "ADD",
      inverted: false,
      maskFeather: 10,
      maskOpacity: 100,
      maskExpansion: 0
    };
    setMasks([...masks, newMask]);
    ae("addMask", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, name: `Mask ${newIndex}` });
  };

  const handleRemoveMask = (maskIdx: number) => {
    setMasks(masks.filter(m => m.index !== maskIdx));
    // execute ExtendScript script to delete
    ae("executeScript", {
      script: `app.project.activeItem.layer(${layer.index}).property('ADBE Mask Parade').property(${maskIdx}).remove();`
    });
  };

  // --- Keyframes scanner ---
  const scanKeyframes = async () => {
    if (!kfPropPath) {
      alert("Please select or enter property path, e.g. 'ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Position'");
      return;
    }
    if (isDemoMode) {
      setKeyframes([
        { index: 1, time: 1.25, value: [540, 540] },
        { index: 2, time: 3.5, value: [1200, 540] },
        { index: 3, time: 7.12, value: [960, 900] }
      ]);
    } else {
      const data = await ae("getKeyframes", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, propertyPath: kfPropPath });
      if (data && data.keyframes) {
        setKeyframes(data.keyframes);
      } else {
        setKeyframes([]);
      }
    }
  };

  const handleRemoveKeyframe = (time: number) => {
    setKeyframes(keyframes.filter(k => k.time !== time));
    ae("removeKeyframeAtTime", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, propertyPath: kfPropPath, time });
  };

  return (
    <div className="layer-accordions flex flex-col gap-2 mt-3 text-white/90">
      {/* 1. Transform & Timing Accordion */}
      <div className={`inline-accordion border transition-all duration-200 rounded-lg overflow-hidden ${
        activeAcc === "transform" ? "border-[#e8a838]/40 bg-[#0c0c10]" : "border-white/5 bg-[#14141a]/45"
      }`}>
        <div
          onClick={() => toggleAccordion("transform")}
          className="acc-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-white/[0.01] hover:bg-white/[0.04] cursor-pointer"
        >
          <span className={`text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wider font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1.5 ${
            activeAcc === "transform" ? "text-[#e8a838]" : "text-white/60"
          }`}>
            <Move className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Transform & Timing Controls
          </span>
          <span className="text-[10px] text-white/40">{activeAcc === "transform" ? "▼" : "▶"}</span>
        </div>

        {activeAcc === "transform" && (
          <div className="acc-body p-4 border-t border-white/5 flex flex-col gap-4">
            {/* Parenting, Blend Mode & Stretch */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-3 gap-3 bg-black/20 p-2.5 rounded-lg border border-white/5">
              <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white/40 uppercase font-sans">Track Parent</span>
                <select
                  value={parentIndex}
                  onChange={(e) => handleParentChange(parseInt(e.target.value))}
                  className="bg-[#0f0f12] text-white text-xs py-1 px-2 rounded outline-none border border-white/5"
                >
                  <option value="0">None</option>
                  {layersList.map(lay => (
                    lay.index !== layer.index && (
                      <option key={lay.index} value={lay.index}>
                        {lay.index}. {lay.name}
                      </option>
                    )
                  ))}
                </select>
              </div>

              <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white/40 uppercase font-sans">Blending Mode</span>
                <select
                  value={blendMode}
                  onChange={(e) => handleBlendChange(e.target.value)}
                  className="bg-[#0f0f12] text-white text-xs py-1 px-2 rounded outline-none border border-white/5"
                >
                  {["Normal", "Darken", "Multiply", "Add", "Screen", "Overlay", "SoftLight", "HardLight", "Difference", "Color", "Luminosity"].map(m => (
                    <option key={m} value={m}>{m}</option>
                  ))}
                </select>
              </div>

              <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white/40 uppercase font-sans">Stretch / Time Stretch</span>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
                  <input
                    type="number"
                    value={stretch}
                    onChange={(e) => handleStretchChange(parseFloat(e.target.value) || 100)}
                    className="w-16 bg-[#0f0f12] text-white text-xs py-1 px-2 rounded outline-none border border-white/5 text-center font-mono"
                  />
                  <button
                    onClick={handleReverseToggle}
                    className={`px-2 py-1 text-[9px] font-bold rounded ${
                      stretch < 0 ? "bg-rose-500/20 border border-rose-500 text-rose-400" : "bg-white/5 text-white/60 hover:text-white"
                    }`}
                  >
                    REV
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Interactive Visual Trackpad Field */}
            <div className="flex flex-col gap-1 bg-[#070709]">
              <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white/40 uppercase font-sans">Visual Touch Trackpad</span>
              <div
                ref={trackpadRef}
                onPointerMove={handleTrackpadPointer}
                onPointerDown={handleTrackpadPointer}
                className="w-full h-28 trackpad rounded-lg relative cursor-crosshair flex items-center justify-center select-none touch-none overflow-hidden"
              >
                <div className="absolute w-4 h-4 border border-[#e8a838]/60 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center pointer-events-none">
                  <span className="w-1 h-1 bg-[#e8a838] rounded-full" />
                </div>
                <span className="text-[10px] text-white/20 select-none">
                  {trackpadMode === "position" && "Drag to fine position"}
                  {trackpadMode === "scale" && "Drag to adjust scale"}
                  {trackpadMode === "rotation" && "Drag to rotate"}
                </span>

                <div className="absolute bottom-2.5 right-3 text-[10px] font-mono text-[#e8a838]">
                  {trackpadMode === "position" && `${posX}, ${posY} px`}
                  {trackpadMode === "scale" && `${scaleX}%, ${scaleY}%`}
                  {trackpadMode === "rotation" && `${rotation} deg`}
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Modify mode controls */}
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mt-1">
                <div className="flex gap-1">
                  {["position", "scale", "rotation"].map((mode) => (
                    <button
                      key={mode}
                      onClick={() => setTrackpadMode(mode as any)}
                      className={`px-2 py-0.5 text-[9px] font-bold uppercase rounded ${
                        trackpadMode === mode ? "bg-[#e8a838] text-black" : "bg-white/5 text-white/50"
                      }`}
                    >
                      {mode}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>

                <div className="flex gap-2 text-[8px] font-mono text-white/20">
                  <span className={isAltPressed ? "text-[#e8a838]" : ""}>ALT (FINE)</span>
                  <span className={isShiftPressed ? "text-[#e8a838]" : ""}>SHIFT (COARSE)</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Transform Sliders Parameters Block */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-2">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-white/40 w-16 uppercase">Position X</span>
                <input
                  type="range"
                  min="0"
                  max="1920"
                  value={posX}
                  onChange={(e) => {
                    const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                    setPosX(v);
                    applyParamChange("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Position", [v, posY]);
                  }}
                  className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
                />
                <span className="w-12 font-mono text-xs text-right text-white/80">{posX}</span>
                <button onClick={() => setParamKeyframe("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Position")} className="text-[10px]">◇</button>
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-white/40 w-16 uppercase">Position Y</span>
                <input
                  type="range"
                  min="0"
                  max="1080"
                  value={posY}
                  onChange={(e) => {
                    const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                    setPosY(v);
                    applyParamChange("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Position", [posX, v]);
                  }}
                  className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
                />
                <span className="w-12 font-mono text-xs text-right text-white/80">{posY}</span>
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-white/40 w-16 uppercase">Scale X</span>
                <input
                  type="range"
                  min="0"
                  max="400"
                  value={scaleX}
                  onChange={(e) => {
                    const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                    setScaleX(v);
                    applyParamChange("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Scale", [v, scaleY]);
                  }}
                  className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
                />
                <span className="w-12 font-mono text-xs text-right text-white/80">{scaleX}%</span>
                <button onClick={() => setParamKeyframe("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Scale")} className="text-[10px]">◇</button>
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-white/40 w-16 uppercase">Rotation</span>
                <input
                  type="range"
                  min="-360"
                  max="360"
                  value={rotation}
                  onChange={(e) => {
                    const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                    setRotation(v);
                    applyParamChange("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Rotate Z", v);
                  }}
                  className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
                />
                <span className="w-12 font-mono text-xs text-right text-white/80">{rotation}°</span>
                <button onClick={() => setParamKeyframe("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Rotate Z")} className="text-[10px]">◇</button>
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-white/40 w-16 uppercase">Opacity</span>
                <input
                  type="range"
                  min="0"
                  max="100"
                  value={opacity}
                  onChange={(e) => {
                    const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                    setOpacity(v);
                    applyParamChange("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Opacity", v);
                  }}
                  className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
                />
                <span className="w-12 font-mono text-xs text-right text-white/80">{opacity}%</span>
                <button onClick={() => setParamKeyframe("ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Opacity")} className="text-[10px]">◇</button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* 2. Effects Accordion */}
      <div className={`inline-accordion border transition-all duration-200 rounded-lg overflow-hidden ${
        activeAcc === "effects" ? "border-[#e8a838]/40 bg-[#0c0c10]" : "border-white/5 bg-[#14141a]/45"
      }`}>
        <div
          onClick={() => toggleAccordion("effects")}
          className="acc-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-white/[0.01] hover:bg-white/[0.04] cursor-pointer"
        >
          <span className={`text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wider font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1.5 ${
            activeAcc === "effects" ? "text-[#e8a838]" : "text-white/60"
          }`}>
            <Sliders className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Effects Management
          </span>
          <span className="text-[10px] text-white/40">{activeAcc === "effects" ? "▼" : "▶"}</span>
        </div>

        {activeAcc === "effects" && (
          <div className="acc-body p-4 border-t border-white/5 flex flex-col gap-3">
            {/* Search input and autocomplete list */}
            <div className="relative">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-[#070709] border border-white/5 rounded-lg px-3 py-1.5 focus-within:border-[#e8a838] focus-within:shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(232,168,56,0.15)] transition-all-300">
                <Search className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-white/30" />
                <input
                  type="text"
                  value={fxQuery}
                  onChange={(e) => setFxQuery(e.target.value)}
                  placeholder="Search & add effect (Glow, Blur...)..."
                  className="bg-transparent border-none text-white text-xs outline-none flex-1 min-width-0 font-sans"
                />
              </div>

              {fxQuery.trim().length > 0 && (
                <div className="absolute top-full left-0 right-0 mt-1 bg-[#121217] border border-white/5 rounded-lg shadow-2xl z-25 py-1.5 max-h-[160px] overflow-y-auto">
                  {effectsPresets
                    .filter(f => f.name.toLowerCase().includes(fxQuery.toLowerCase()))
                    .map(f => (
                      <button
                        key={f.matchName}
                        onClick={() => handleAddEffect(f.matchName, f.name)}
                        className="w-full px-4 py-2 text-left text-xs text-white/70 hover:bg-[#e8a838]/10 hover:text-[#e8a838] transition-colors"
                      >
                        + Add {f.name}
                      </button>
                    ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* Effects parades list */}
            <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-2">
              {fxList.length === 0 ? (
                <span className="text-[11px] text-white/30 text-center py-4 font-sans italic">No effects on this layer.</span>
              ) : (
                fxList.map(fx => (
                  <div key={fx.index} className="bg-black/30 border border-white/5 rounded-lg p-2.5">
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-1.5">
                      <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-white/90">{fx.name}</span>
                      <button
                        onClick={() => handleRemoveEffect(fx.index)}
                        className="p-1 rounded text-rose-400 hover:bg-rose-500/10 transition-colors"
                        title="Delete Effect"
                      >
                        <Trash2 className="w-3 h-3" />
                      </button>
                    </div>

                    {/* Simple conditional sliders Mock */}
                    {fx.name === "Gaussian Blur" && (
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-1">
                        <span className="text-[9px] font-mono text-white/40 w-16">Blurriness</span>
                        <input
                          type="range"
                          min="0"
                          max="150"
                          defaultValue="25"
                          className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
                        />
                      </div>
                    )}
                    {fx.name === "Glow" && (
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mt-1">
                        <span className="text-[9px] font-mono text-white/40 w-16">Intensity</span>
                        <input
                          type="range"
                          min="0"
                          max="10"
                          step="0.1"
                          value={glowIntensity}
                          onChange={(e) => setGlowIntensity(parseFloat(e.target.value))}
                          className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
                        />
                        <span className="text-[10px] text-white/60 font-mono w-6 text-right">{glowIntensity.toFixed(1)}</span>
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                ))
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* 3. Styling & Audio Accordion */}
      <div className={`inline-accordion border transition-all duration-200 rounded-lg overflow-hidden ${
        activeAcc === "styling" ? "border-[#e8a838]/40 bg-[#0c0c10]" : "border-white/5 bg-[#14141a]/45"
      }`}>
        <div
          onClick={() => toggleAccordion("styling")}
          className="acc-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-white/[0.01] hover:bg-white/[0.04] cursor-pointer"
        >
          <span className={`text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wider font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1.5 ${
            activeAcc === "styling" ? "text-[#e8a838]" : "text-white/60"
          }`}>
            <Volume2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Styling & Audio Volume
          </span>
          <span className="text-[10px] text-white/40">{activeAcc === "styling" ? "▼" : "▶"}</span>
        </div>

        {activeAcc === "styling" && (
          <div className="acc-body p-4 border-t border-white/5 flex flex-col gap-4">
            {/* Custom Audio Volume Decibel adjustment tracker */}
            {(layer.hasAudio || layer.layerType === "av" || isDemoMode) && (
              <div className="bg-[#4caf50]/5 border border-[#4caf50]/20 rounded-lg p-3">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                  <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-emerald-400 font-sans tracking-tight flex items-center gap-1">
                    <Volume2 className="w-3 h-3 text-[#4caf50]" /> DECIBEL AUDIO LEVELS
                  </span>
                  <span className="text-[11px] font-mono text-[#e8a838] font-bold">
                    {audioDb <= -48 ? "MUTE (-INF)" : `${audioDb.toFixed(1)} dB`}
                  </span>
                </div>
                <input
                  type="range"
                  min="-48"
                  max="12"
                  step="0.5"
                  value={audioDb}
                  onChange={handleVolumeChange}
                  className="w-full accent-emerald-500"
                />
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Shapers Styling Custom Colors swatches (Fill, Stroke, Drop Shadow) */}
            {(layer.layerType === "shape" || layer.layerType === "text" || isDemoMode) ? (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                {/* Fill Block */}
                <div className="bg-black/30 border border-white/5 rounded-lg p-2.5">
                  <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white/40 uppercase font-sans mb-1.5 block">Fill Properties</span>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <div
                      className="w-7 h-7 rounded-sm border border-white/10 cursor-pointer flex-shrink-0"
                      style={{ backgroundColor: fillColor }}
                      onClick={() => document.getElementById(`inlineFillNative-${layer.index}`)?.click()}
                    />
                    <input
                      type="color"
                      id={`inlineFillNative-${layer.index}`}
                      value={fillColor}
                      onChange={(e) => {
                        setFillColor(e.target.value);
                        const rgb = hexToRgb(e.target.value);
                        applyParamChange("ADBE Root Vectors Group/Rectangle/Fill/Color", [rgb.r / 255, rgb.g / 255, rgb.b / 255]);
                      }}
                      className="hidden"
                    />
                    <span className="text-xs font-mono text-white/70">{fillColor.toUpperCase()}</span>
                  </div>
                </div>

                {/* Stroke properties */}
                <div className="bg-black/30 border border-white/5 rounded-lg p-2.5">
                  <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white/40 uppercase font-sans mb-1.5 block">Stroke (Outline)</span>
                  <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                      <div
                        className="w-7 h-7 rounded-sm border border-white/10 cursor-pointer flex-shrink-0"
                        style={{ backgroundColor: strokeColor }}
                        onClick={() => document.getElementById(`inlineStrokeNative-${layer.index}`)?.click()}
                      />
                      <input
                        type="color"
                        id={`inlineStrokeNative-${layer.index}`}
                        value={strokeColor}
                        onChange={(e) => {
                          setStrokeColor(e.target.value);
                          const rgb = hexToRgb(e.target.value);
                          applyParamChange("ADBE Root Vectors Group/Rectangle/Stroke/Color", [rgb.r / 255, rgb.g / 255, rgb.b / 255]);
                        }}
                        className="hidden"
                      />
                      <span className="text-xs font-mono text-white/70">{strokeColor.toUpperCase()}</span>
                    </div>

                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                      <span className="text-[9px] text-white/40 font-mono">Width</span>
                      <input
                        type="range"
                        min="0"
                        max="20"
                        value={strokeWidth}
                        onChange={(e) => {
                          const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                          setStrokeWidth(v);
                          applyParamChange("ADBE Root Vectors Group/Rectangle/Stroke/Width", v);
                        }}
                        className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
                      />
                      <span className="text-xs font-mono w-4 text-right">{strokeWidth}</span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>

                {/* Drop shadow effects slider */}
                <div className="bg-black/30 border border-white/5 rounded-lg p-2.5 sm:col-span-2">
                  <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white/40 uppercase font-sans mb-2 block">Drop Shadow FX Params (Simulated)</span>
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3">
                    <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                      <span className="text-[9px] text-white/40 font-mono">Opacity</span>
                      <input
                        type="range"
                        min="0"
                        max="255"
                        value={shadowOpacity}
                        onChange={(e) => setShadowOpacity(parseInt(e.target.value))}
                        className="accent-[#e8a838]"
                      />
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                      <span className="text-[9px] text-white/40 font-mono">Distance</span>
                      <input
                        type="range"
                        min="0"
                        max="100"
                        value={shadowDistance}
                        onChange={(e) => setShadowDistance(parseInt(e.target.value))}
                        className="accent-[#e8a838]"
                      />
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex flex-col gap-1">
                      <span className="text-[9px] text-white/40 font-mono">Softness</span>
                      <input
                        type="range"
                        min="0"
                        max="100"
                        value={shadowSoftness}
                        onChange={(e) => setShadowSoftness(parseInt(e.target.value))}
                        className="accent-[#e8a838]"
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <span className="text-[11px] text-white/30 text-center py-4 font-sans italic">
                Only shape, solid or text layers support custom border stroke & fill swatches.
              </span>
            )}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* 4. Masking Accordion */}
      <div className={`inline-accordion border transition-all duration-200 rounded-lg overflow-hidden ${
        activeAcc === "masks" ? "border-[#e8a838]/40 bg-[#0c0c10]" : "border-white/5 bg-[#14141a]/45"
      }`}>
        <div
          onClick={() => toggleAccordion("masks")}
          className="acc-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-white/[0.01] hover:bg-white/[0.04] cursor-pointer"
        >
          <span className={`text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wider font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1.5 ${
            activeAcc === "masks" ? "text-[#e8a838]" : "text-white/60"
          }`}>
            <Eye className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Masking Parameters
          </span>
          <span className="text-[10px] text-white/40">{activeAcc === "masks" ? "▼" : "▶"}</span>
        </div>

        {activeAcc === "masks" && (
          <div className="acc-body p-4 border-t border-white/5 flex flex-col gap-3">
            <button
              onClick={handleAddMask}
              className="py-1 px-2 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-[10px] font-semibold tracking-wider text-[#e8a838] rounded-md transition-all self-start flex items-center gap-1"
            >
              <Plus className="w-3 h-3" /> Add Mask
            </button>

            <div className="flex flex-col gap-2.5 mt-1">
              {masks.length === 0 ? (
                <span className="text-[11px] text-white/30 text-center py-4 font-sans italic">No active masks on this layer.</span>
              ) : (
                masks.map(m => (
                  <div key={m.index} className="bg-black/30 border border-white/5 rounded-lg p-3">
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2 pb-1.5 border-b border-white/5">
                      <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-white/80">{m.name}</span>
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <select
                          value={m.maskMode}
                          onChange={(e) => {
                            const updated = masks.map(x => x.index === m.index ? { ...x, maskMode: e.target.value } : x);
                            setMasks(updated);
                            ae("setMaskMode", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, maskIndex: m.index, mode: e.target.value });
                          }}
                          className="bg-[#0f0f12] text-white text-[10px] font-bold py-0.5 px-2 rounded outline-none border border-white/5 uppercase"
                        >
                          {["Add", "Subtract", "Intersect", "Difference", "None"].map(item => (
                            <option key={item} value={item.toUpperCase()}>{item}</option>
                          ))}
                        </select>

                        <button
                          onClick={() => handleRemoveMask(m.index)}
                          className="p-1 rounded text-rose-400 hover:bg-rose-500/10 transition-colors"
                        >
                          <Trash2 className="w-3 h-3" />
                        </button>
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3.5">
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <span className="text-[9px] text-white/40 font-mono w-14">Opacity</span>
                        <input
                          type="range"
                          min="0"
                          max="100"
                          value={m.maskOpacity}
                          onChange={(e) => {
                            const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                            const updated = masks.map(x => x.index === m.index ? { ...x, maskOpacity: v } : x);
                            setMasks(updated);
                            ae("setMaskProperty", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, maskIndex: m.index, opacity: v });
                          }}
                          className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
                        />
                        <span className="text-[10px] text-white/60 font-mono w-5 text-right">{m.maskOpacity}%</span>
                      </div>

                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <span className="text-[9px] text-white/40 font-mono w-14">Expansion</span>
                        <input
                          type="range"
                          min="-200"
                          max="200"
                          value={m.maskExpansion}
                          onChange={(e) => {
                            const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                            const updated = masks.map(x => x.index === m.index ? { ...x, maskExpansion: v } : x);
                            setMasks(updated);
                            ae("setMaskProperty", { compIndex: null, layerIndex: layer.index, maskIndex: m.index, expansion: v });
                          }}
                          className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
                        />
                        <span className="text-[10px] text-white/60 font-mono w-5 text-right">{m.maskExpansion}</span>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* 5. Keyframes Accordion */}
      <div className={`inline-accordion border transition-all duration-200 rounded-lg overflow-hidden ${
        activeAcc === "keyframes" ? "border-[#e8a838]/40 bg-[#0c0c10]" : "border-white/5 bg-[#14141a]/45"
      }`}>
        <div
          onClick={() => toggleAccordion("keyframes")}
          className="acc-header flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-white/[0.01] hover:bg-white/[0.04] cursor-pointer"
        >
          <span className={`text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wider font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1.5 ${
            activeAcc === "keyframes" ? "text-[#e8a838]" : "text-white/60"
          }`}>
            <Key className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Keyframe parade
          </span>
          <span className="text-[10px] text-white/40">{activeAcc === "keyframes" ? "▼" : "▶"}</span>
        </div>

        {activeAcc === "keyframes" && (
          <div className="acc-body p-4 border-t border-white/5 flex flex-col gap-3">
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <select
                value={kfPropPath}
                onChange={(e) => setKfPropPath(e.target.value)}
                className="bg-[#0f0f12] text-white text-xs py-1.5 px-3 rounded-lg outline-none border border-white/5 flex-1 cursor-pointer"
              >
                <option value="">Select Property to Scan...</option>
                <option value="ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Position">Transform Position</option>
                <option value="ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Scale">Transform Scale</option>
                <option value="ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Rotate Z">Transform Rotation</option>
                <option value="ADBE Transform Group/ADBE Opacity">Transform Opacity</option>
              </select>
              <button
                onClick={scanKeyframes}
                className="px-3 py-1.5 bg-[#e8a838] text-[#070709] text-xs font-bold rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e8a838]/90 transition-all font-sans"
              >
                Scan Keys
              </button>
            </div>

            <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 mt-2">
              {keyframes.length === 0 ? (
                <span className="text-[11px] text-white/30 text-center py-4 font-sans italic">No keyframes scanner results.</span>
              ) : (
                <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5 max-h-[180px] overflow-y-auto pr-1">
                  {keyframes.map(kf => (
                    <div key={kf.index} className="flex items-center justify-between bg-black/20 px-3 py-2 rounded border border-white/5 font-mono text-xs">
                      <span className="text-[#e8a838] font-bold">T: {kf.time.toFixed(3)}s</span>
                      <span className="text-white/50 truncate max-w-[200px]">{JSON.stringify(kf.value)}</span>
                      <button
                        onClick={() => handleRemoveKeyframe(kf.time)}
                        className="text-rose-400 font-sans text-[10px] hover:underline"
                      >
                        Remove
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

import React from "react";
import { Layer } from "../types";

interface ShapesPanelProps {
  layerList: Layer[];
  selectedLayerIndex: number | null;
  onSelectLayer: (idx: number) => void;
  onAddShape: (type: "Rectangle" | "Ellipse") => void;
}

export const ShapesPanel: React.FC<ShapesPanelProps> = ({
  layerList,
  selectedLayerIndex,
  onSelectLayer,
  onAddShape
}) => {
  const shapeLayers = layerList.filter(l => l.layerType === "shape");

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between bg-[#121217] border border-white/5 p-4 rounded-xl">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <span className="text-xs text-white/50 font-sans font-bold uppercase">Shape Target</span>
          <select
            value={selectedLayerIndex || ""}
            onChange={(e) => onSelectLayer(parseInt(e.target.value) || 0)}
            className="sel bg-[#070709] border border-white/5 text-white text-xs px-2.5 py-1.5 rounded-lg outline-none cursor-pointer min-w-[180px]"
          >
            <option value="">Select Shape Layer...</option>
            {shapeLayers.map(l => (
              <option key={l.index} value={l.index}>
                {l.index}. {l.name}
              </option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>

        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <button
            onClick={() => onAddShape("Rectangle")}
            className="px-3 py-1.5 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-white border border-white/5 rounded-lg text-xs"
          >
            + Rectangle Path
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => onAddShape("Ellipse")}
            className="px-3 py-1.5 bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-white border border-white/5 rounded-lg text-xs"
          >
            + Ellipse Path
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="bg-[#121217] border border-white/5 p-6 rounded-xl flex flex-col items-center text-center">
        <span className="text-3xl mb-2">⬠</span>
        <h4 className="text-sm font-semibold text-white/90">Shape Layer Presets</h4>
        <p className="text-xs text-white/40 max-w-sm mt-1 mb-4">
          Select an active shape layer above to append vector paths recursively, or edit fill swatches from the layers inline drawer styling panel.
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

FILE: src/components/TextPanel.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState } from "react";
import { Layer } from "../types";
import { Type, Play } from "lucide-react";

interface TextPanelProps {
  layerList: Layer[];
  selectedLayerIndex: number | null;
  onSelectLayer: (idx: number) => void;
  isDemoMode: boolean;
  ae: (action: string, params?: any) => Promise<any>;
}

export const TextPanel: React.FC<TextPanelProps> = ({
  layerList,
  selectedLayerIndex,
  onSelectLayer,
  isDemoMode,
  ae
}) => {
  const textLayers = layerList.filter(l => l.layerType === "text");
  const [sourceText, setSourceText] = useState("Touch Tools");
  const [fontSize, setFontSize] = useState(72);

  const handleUpdateText = () => {
    if (!selectedLayerIndex) return;
    if (isDemoMode) {
      alert(`Simulated text update: "${sourceText}"`);
    } else {
      ae("executeScript", {
        script: `app.project.activeItem.layer(${selectedLayerIndex}).property("ADBE Text Properties").property("ADBE Text Document").setValue(new TextDocument("${sourceText}"));`
      });
    }
  };

  const applyTextChange = (prop: string, v: number) => {
    if (!isDemoMode && selectedLayerIndex) {
      ae("setValue", {
        compIndex: null,
        layerIndex: selectedLayerIndex,
        propertyPath: `ADBE Text Properties/ADBE Text Document/${prop}`,
        value: v
      });
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 bg-[#121217] border border-white/5 p-4 rounded-xl">
        <span className="text-xs text-white/50 font-sans font-bold uppercase">Text Layer</span>
        <select
          value={selectedLayerIndex || ""}
          onChange={(e) => onSelectLayer(parseInt(e.target.value) || 0)}
          className="sel bg-[#070709] border border-white/5 text-white text-xs px-2.5 py-1.5 rounded-lg outline-none cursor-pointer min-w-[200px]"
        >
          <option value="">Select Text Layer...</option>
          {textLayers.map(l => (
            <option key={l.index} value={l.index}>
              {l.index}. {l.name}
            </option>
          ))}
        </select>
      </div>

      <div className="bg-[#121217] border border-white/5 p-5 rounded-xl flex flex-col gap-4">
        <h3 className="text-xs font-bold tracking-wider text-[#e8a838] font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1.5">
          <Type className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> Source Document Text properties
        </h3>

        <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col gap-4">
          <div className="flex flex-col gap-1.5 max-w-md">
            <span className="text-[10px] text-white/40 uppercase font-sans font-bold">Source Text Input</span>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <input
                type="text"
                value={sourceText}
                onChange={(e) => setSourceText(e.target.value)}
                className="bg-[#0f0f12] text-white border border-white/5 rounded-lg px-3 py-1.5 text-xs outline-none flex-1 focus:border-[#e8a838]"
              />
              <button
                onClick={handleUpdateText}
                className="px-3.5 py-1.5 bg-[#e8a838] text-black text-xs font-bold rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e8a838]/90 transition-all font-sans"
              >
                Update
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 max-w-md mt-2">
            <span className="text-[10px] font-mono text-white/40 w-24 uppercase">Font Size</span>
            <input
              type="range"
              min="8"
              max="200"
              value={fontSize}
              onChange={(e) => {
                const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                setFontSize(v);
                applyTextChange("fontSize", v);
              }}
              className="flex-1 accent-[#e8a838]"
            />
            <span className="w-12 font-mono text-xs text-right text-white/80">{fontSize} pt</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};
