FILE: src/components/Toolbar.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState } from "react";
import { CompItem } from "../types";
import { RefreshCw, ZoomIn, ZoomOut, Maximize2, Grid, ChevronDown, Plus, PlusCircle, AlignLeft, Video, Lightbulb } from "lucide-react";

interface ToolbarProps {
  compositions: CompItem[];
  selectedCompIndex: number | null;
  onSelectComp: (index: number) => void;
  onRefresh: () => void;
  onCanvasCommand: (cmd: "zoomIn" | "zoomOut" | "fit" | "grid") => void;
  onCreateLayer: (type: "solid" | "shape" | "text" | "null" | "camera" | "light", arg?: any) => void;
  compSettingsOpen: boolean;
  onToggleCompSettings: () => void;
}

export const Toolbar: React.FC<ToolbarProps> = ({
  compositions,
  selectedCompIndex,
  onSelectComp,
  onRefresh,
  onCanvasCommand,
  onCreateLayer,
  compSettingsOpen,
  onToggleCompSettings
}) => {
  const [isShapeMenuOpen, setIsShapeMenuOpen] = useState(false);

  const handleCreateShape = (type: string) => {
    onCreateLayer("shape", type);
    setIsShapeMenuOpen(false);
  };

  return (
    <section className="bg-[#070709] border-b border-white/5 py-2.5 px-4 flex-shrink-0">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-4">
        {/* Left Side: Comp dropdown + manual trigger + Settings toggle */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-grow sm:flex-grow-0">
          <select
            value={selectedCompIndex || ""}
            onChange={(e) => onSelectComp(parseInt(e.target.value) || 0)}
            className="sel bg-[#0f0f12] text-white text-xs border border-white/5 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg outline-none cursor-pointer min-w-[200px]"
          >
            <option value="">Select Composition...</option>
            {compositions.map((comp) => (
              <option key={comp.index} value={comp.index}>
                {comp.index}. {comp.name} ({comp.width}×{comp.height})
              </option>
            ))}
          </select>
          
          <button
            onClick={onRefresh}
            className="p-1.5 rounded-lg bg-[#121217] hover:bg-white/5 border border-white/5 text-white/60 hover:text-white transition-all duration-300"
            title="Refresh All Compositions & Layers"
          >
            <RefreshCw className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
          </button>

          <button
            onClick={onToggleCompSettings}
            className={`px-3 py-1.5 border hover:border-amber/40 bg-[#121217] text-[10px] font-bold text-[#e8a838] rounded-lg transition-all flex items-center gap-1.5 uppercase tracking-wide cursor-pointer select-none ${
              compSettingsOpen ? "bg-[#e8a838]/10 border-amber/50 shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(232,168,56,0.15)]" : "border-amber/20 hover:bg-white/5"
            }`}
            title="Configure active composition settings"
          >
            <span>⚙️ settings</span>
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Center: Canvas utility buttons */}
        <div className="flex items-center bg-[#121217] border border-white/5 rounded-lg p-0.5 gap-0.5" title="Canvas View Tools">
          <button
            onClick={() => onCanvasCommand("zoomIn")}
            className="p-1.5 rounded text-white/50 hover:text-white hover:bg-white/5 transition-all text-xs flex items-center gap-1 font-sans"
            title="Zoom In"
          >
            <ZoomIn className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => onCanvasCommand("zoomOut")}
            className="p-1.5 rounded text-white/50 hover:text-white hover:bg-white/5 transition-all text-xs flex items-center gap-1 font-sans"
            title="Zoom Out"
          >
            <ZoomOut className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => onCanvasCommand("fit")}
            className="p-1.5 rounded text-white/50 hover:text-white hover:bg-white/5 transition-all text-xs flex items-center gap-1 font-sans"
            title="Fit Canvas"
          >
            <Maximize2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => onCanvasCommand("grid")}
            className="p-1.5 rounded text-white/50 hover:text-white hover:bg-white/5 transition-all text-xs flex items-center gap-1 font-sans"
            title="Toggle Grid / Transparency"
          >
            <Grid className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Right Side: Quick layer creators */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 flex-wrap">
          <button
            onClick={() => onCreateLayer("solid")}
            className="px-2.5 py-1.5 bg-[#121217] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/80 border border-white/5 hover:border-white/10 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wider rounded-md transition-all font-sans uppercase"
          >
            + Solid
          </button>

          {/* Collapsible Shape Creator Menu */}
          <div className="relative">
            <button
              onClick={() => setIsShapeMenuOpen(!isShapeMenuOpen)}
              className="px-2.5 py-1.5 bg-[#121217] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/80 border border-white/5 hover:border-white/10 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wider rounded-md transition-all font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1"
            >
              + Shape <ChevronDown className="w-2.5 h-2.5" />
            </button>
            {isShapeMenuOpen && (
              <>
                <div className="fixed inset-0 z-40" onClick={() => setIsShapeMenuOpen(false)} />
                <div className="absolute top-full left-0 mt-1 bg-[#121217] border border-white/5 rounded-lg shadow-2xl z-50 py-1.5 min-w-[130px] flex flex-col overflow-hidden animate-fade-in">
                  {["Rectangle", "Ellipse", "Polygon", "Star", "Line"].map((shape) => (
                    <button
                      key={shape}
                      onClick={() => handleCreateShape(shape)}
                      className="px-4 py-2 text-left text-xs text-white/70 hover:bg-[#e8a838]/10 hover:text-[#e8a838] transition-colors"
                    >
                      {shape === "Rectangle" && "■ "}
                      {shape === "Ellipse" && "● "}
                      {shape}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </>
            )}
          </div>

          <button
            onClick={() => onCreateLayer("text")}
            className="px-2.5 py-1.5 bg-[#121217] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/80 border border-white/5 hover:border-white/10 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wider rounded-md transition-all font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1"
          >
            <AlignLeft className="w-3 h-3 text-[#e8a838]" /> Text
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => onCreateLayer("null")}
            className="px-2.5 py-1.5 bg-[#121217] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/80 border border-white/5 hover:border-white/10 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wider rounded-md transition-all font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1"
          >
            <PlusCircle className="w-3 h-3 text-white/40" /> Null
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => onCreateLayer("camera")}
            className="px-2.5 py-1.5 bg-[#121217] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/80 border border-white/5 hover:border-white/10 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wider rounded-md transition-all font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1"
          >
            <Video className="w-3 h-3 text-white/50" /> Cam
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => onCreateLayer("light")}
            className="px-2.5 py-1.5 bg-[#121217] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/80 border border-white/5 hover:border-white/10 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-wider rounded-md transition-all font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1"
          >
            <Lightbulb className="w-3 h-3 text-[#ffc107]" /> Light
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  );
};


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/components/TransportBar.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useRef, MouseEvent, TouchEvent } from "react";
import { formatTimecode } from "../utils";
import { Play, Pause, ChevronLeft, ChevronRight, SkipBack, SkipForward } from "lucide-react";

interface TransportBarProps {
  isPlaying: boolean;
  onPlayToggle: () => void;
  currentTime: number;
  duration: number;
  fps: number;
  onScrubTime: (newTime: number) => void;
  onPrevFrame: () => void;
  onNextFrame: () => void;
  onPrevKeyframe: () => void;
  onNextKeyframe: () => void;
  onGoStart: () => void;
  onGoEnd: () => void;
}

export const TransportBar: React.FC<TransportBarProps> = ({
  isPlaying,
  onPlayToggle,
  currentTime,
  duration,
  fps,
  onScrubTime,
  onPrevFrame,
  onNextFrame,
  onPrevKeyframe,
  onNextKeyframe,
  onGoStart,
  onGoEnd
}) => {
  const trackRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const calculateScrubTime = (clientX: number) => {
    if (!trackRef.current || duration <= 0) return;
    const rect = trackRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    const x = clientX - rect.left;
    const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, x / rect.width));
    onScrubTime(pct * duration);
  };

  const handlePointerDown = (e: React.PointerEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    trackRef.current?.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    calculateScrubTime(e.clientX);
  };

  const handlePointerMove = (e: React.PointerEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    if (trackRef.current && trackRef.current.hasPointerCapture(e.pointerId)) {
      calculateScrubTime(e.clientX);
    }
  };

  const handlePointerUp = (e: React.PointerEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
    trackRef.current?.releasePointerCapture(e.pointerId);
  };

  const currentFrame = Math.round(currentTime * fps);
  const totalFrames = Math.round(duration * fps);
  const percent = duration > 0 ? (currentTime / duration) * 100 : 0;

  return (
    <section className="bg-[#121217] border-b border-white/5 py-2.5 px-4 flex-shrink-0">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto flex flex-col md:flex-row items-center gap-3 justify-between">
        {/* Playback Buttons Group */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
          <button
            onClick={onGoStart}
            className="p-1.5 rounded bg-white/[0.02] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/50 hover:text-white transition-all text-xs"
            title="Go to Start"
          >
            <SkipBack className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
          </button>
          
          <button
            onClick={onPrevKeyframe}
            className="p-1.5 rounded bg-white/[0.02] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/50 hover:text-[#e8a838] transition-all text-[10px] font-sans flex items-center gap-0.5"
            title="Prev Keyframe"
          >
            ◇⏮
          </button>

          <button
            onClick={onPrevFrame}
            className="p-1.5 rounded bg-white/[0.02] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/50 hover:text-white transition-all text-xs"
            title="Prev Frame"
          >
            <ChevronLeft className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>

          <button
            onClick={onPlayToggle}
            className={`p-2 rounded-lg transition-all text-xs ${
              isPlaying
                ? "bg-[#e8a838]/10 text-[#e8a838] border border-[#e8a838]"
                : "bg-[#e8a838] hover:bg-[#e8a838]/90 text-[#070709]"
            }`}
            title={isPlaying ? "Pause" : "Play"}
          >
            {isPlaying ? <Pause className="w-4 h-4" /> : <Play className="w-4 h-4 fill-current" />}
          </button>

          <button
            onClick={onNextFrame}
            className="p-1.5 rounded bg-white/[0.02] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/50 hover:text-white transition-all text-xs"
            title="Next Frame"
          >
            <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4" />
          </button>

          <button
            onClick={onNextKeyframe}
            className="p-1.5 rounded bg-white/[0.02] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/50 hover:text-[#e8a838] transition-all text-[10px] font-sans flex items-center gap-0.5"
            title="Next Keyframe"
          >
            ⏭◇
          </button>

          <button
            onClick={onGoEnd}
            className="p-1.5 rounded bg-white/[0.02] hover:bg-white/5 text-white/50 hover:text-white transition-all text-xs"
            title="Go to End"
          >
            <SkipForward className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Timecode display */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
          <span className="text-[#e8a838] font-mono font-bold text-base tracking-widest bg-[#070709]/80 px-3 py-1 rounded-md border border-white/5">
            {formatTimecode(currentTime, fps)}
          </span>
        </div>

        {/* Scrubber tracker (Flexible width) */}
        <div className="flex-1 w-full flex items-center gap-3">
          <div
            ref={trackRef}
            onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}
            onPointerMove={handlePointerMove}
            onPointerUp={handlePointerUp}
            className="flex-1 h-5 flex items-center cursor-ew-resize relative touch-none select-none"
          >
            {/* Background track */}
            <div className="w-full h-1.5 bg-white/10 rounded-full relative">
              {/* Active fill */}
              <div
                className="absolute top-0 left-0 h-full bg-[#e8a838] rounded-full shadow-[0_0_8px_rgba(232,168,56,0.2)]"
                style={{ width: `${percent}%` }}
              />
              {/* Scrubber pointer handle */}
              <div
                className="absolute top-1/2 w-3.5 h-3.5 bg-white border border-[#e8a838] rounded-full shadow-[0_1px_4px_rgba(0,0,0,0.5)] transform -translate-x-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 transition-transform hover:scale-125 hover:bg-[#e8a838] cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing"
                style={{ left: `${percent}%` }}
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Frame statistics indicator */}
        <div className="text-right flex-shrink-0 min-w-[70px]">
          <span className="text-[11px] font-mono text-white/40 tracking-wider">
            {currentFrame} / {totalFrames} F
          </span>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  );
};

FILE: src/components/XModePanel.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------

import React, { useState, useEffect } from "react";
import { Terminal, Play, RotateCcw, Trash2, Download, HelpCircle, Activity, CheckCircle, AlertTriangle, RefreshCw, Cpu, HardDrive, Shield } from "lucide-react";
import { BRIDGE_JSX_CONTENT } from "../utils/bridgeScript";

interface XModePanelProps {
  isDemoMode: boolean;
  ae: (action: string, params?: any) => Promise<any>;
}

export const XModePanel: React.FC<XModePanelProps> = ({ isDemoMode, ae }) => {
  const [script, setScript] = useState("// Write ExtendScript here...\nvar comp = app.project.activeItem;\nif (comp) {\n  'Composition: ' + comp.name + ' with ' + comp.numLayers + ' layers';\n} else {\n  'No active composition found';\n}");
  const [output, setOutput] = useState<string>("// Output log console. Run a script above to evaluate.");
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [isError, setIsError] = useState(false);

  // Live Diagnostics Telemetry state
  const [diagnostics, setDiagnostics] = useState<any>(null);
  const [isRefreshingDiag, setIsRefreshingDiag] = useState(false);

  const fetchDiagnostics = async () => {
    setIsRefreshingDiag(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetch("/api/diagnostics");
      if (res.ok) {
        const data = await res.json();
        setDiagnostics(data);
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.warn("Diagnostics API standby/offline (normal in demo or sandbox bounds):", err);
    } finally {
      setIsRefreshingDiag(false);
    }
  };

  // Poll diagnostics periodically every 5000ms
  useEffect(() => {
    fetchDiagnostics();
    const interval = setInterval(fetchDiagnostics, 5000);
    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, []);

  const handleDownloadBridge = () => {
    try {
      // Direct browser-side Blob generation ensures download ALWAYS succeeds as a client feature
      const blob = new Blob([BRIDGE_JSX_CONTENT], { type: "text/javascript" });
      const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      const link = document.createElement("a");
      link.href = url;
      link.download = "bridge.jsx";
      document.body.appendChild(link);
      link.click();
      document.body.removeChild(link);
      URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    } catch (err) {
      // Fallback: direct server route
      window.open("/api/download-bridge", "_blank");
    }
  };

  const handleRunScript = async () => {
    if (!script.trim()) return;
    setIsLoading(true);
    setIsError(false);
    
    if (isDemoMode) {
      setTimeout(() => {
        setIsLoading(false);
        try {
          if (script.includes("app.project.activeItem")) {
            setOutput("Composition: Main Intro Comp with 5 layers");
          } else {
            setOutput("(Simulated execution successful without return value)");
          }
        } catch(e: any) {
          setIsError(true);
          setOutput("ERROR: " + e.message);
        }
      }, 400);
    } else {
      const res = await ae("executeScript", { script });
      setIsLoading(false);
      if (!res) {
        setIsError(true);
        setOutput("Error: No bridge responder WebSocket connected. Open bridge.jsx in After Effects.");
      } else if (res.error) {
        setIsError(true);
        setOutput("EXTENDSCRIPT ERROR: " + res.error);
      } else {
        setOutput(res.result || "(Evaluate completed, return undefined)");
      }
      // Instantly trigger diagnostics update
      fetchDiagnostics();
    }
  };

  const clearScript = () => {
    setScript("");
  };

  const clearOutput = () => {
    setOutput("// Console logs cleared.");
    setIsError(false);
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 h-full min-h-[300px]">
      {/* After Effects Connection Assistance Panel */}
      <div className="bg-[#121217] border border-[#e8a838]/20 rounded-xl p-4 flex flex-col md:flex-row items-start md:items-center justify-between gap-4">
        <div className="flex gap-3 items-start">
          <div className="p-2 rounded-lg bg-[#e8a838]/10 text-[#e8a838] flex-shrink-0">
            <HelpCircle className="w-5 h-5" />
          </div>
          <div>
            <h4 className="text-xs font-bold text-white uppercase tracking-wider">After Effects Connection Help</h4>
            <p className="text-[11px] text-white/50 mt-1 max-w-2xl leading-relaxed">
              If the <code className="text-[#e8a838] bg-[#070709] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-mono text-[10px]">bridge.jsx</code> script file is missing in your downloaded ZIP, download it instantly right here. Enable script network access in After Effects (<span className="text-white/70">Preferences &gt; Scripting &gt; Allow Scripts to Write Files...</span>) and execute via <span className="font-semibold text-white/70">File &gt; Scripts &gt; Run Script File...</span> to link!
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={handleDownloadBridge}
          className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2.5 bg-[#e8a838] text-black text-xs font-bold rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e8a838]/90 transition-all font-sans whitespace-nowrap shadow-[0_0_12px_rgba(232,168,56,0.15)] select-none hover:scale-[1.02] active:scale-[0.98]"
        >
          <Download className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> DOWNLOAD BRIDGE.JSX
        </button>
      </div>

      <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-white/5 pb-2 flex-shrink-0">
        <h3 className="text-xs font-bold tracking-wider text-[#e8a838] font-sans uppercase flex items-center gap-1.5">
          <Terminal className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> ExtendScript Developer Console
        </h3>
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <button
            onClick={clearScript}
            className="p-1 px-2.5 rounded bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-white/50 hover:text-white transition-all text-[10px] font-sans flex items-center gap-1"
          >
            <RotateCcw className="w-3 h-3" /> Clear Editor
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={clearOutput}
            className="p-1 px-2.5 rounded bg-white/5 hover:bg-white/10 text-white/50 hover:text-white transition-all text-[10px] font-sans flex items-center gap-1"
          >
            <Trash2 className="w-3 h-3" /> Clear Output
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={handleRunScript}
            disabled={isLoading}
            className="px-3 py-1 bg-[#e8a838] text-black text-xs font-bold rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e8a838]/90 transition-all font-sans flex items-center gap-1 disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            <Play className="w-3 h-3 fill-current" /> {isLoading ? "EVALUATING..." : "RUN SCRIPT"}
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        {/* Editor */}
        <textarea
          value={script}
          onChange={(e) => setScript(e.target.value)}
          spellCheck={false}
          className="bg-[#0f0f12] text-white p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 font-mono text-xs leading-relaxed outline-none focus:border-[#e8a838] resize-none h-[220px]"
        />

        {/* Output console */}
        <div className="bg-[#070709] border border-white/5 rounded-xl p-4 flex flex-col overflow-hidden h-[220px]">
          <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white/30 uppercase tracking-widest font-sans mb-1.5 flex-shrink-0">
            Console Feedback Logs
          </span>
          <pre className={`flex-1 overflow-y-auto font-mono text-xs whitespace-pre-wrap ${
            isError ? "text-rose-400" : "text-emerald-400"
          }`}>
            {output}
          </pre>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* NEW SYSTEM DIAGNOSTIC PANEL ELEMENT */}
      <div className="border border-white/5 bg-[#0b0b0e] rounded-xl p-4 mt-2">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-white/5 pb-2 mb-3">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <Activity className="w-4 h-4 text-[#e8a838] animate-pulse" />
            <span className="text-xs font-bold text-white uppercase tracking-wider font-sans">
              System Diagnostics Telemetry
            </span>
            <span className="text-[9px] bg-white/5 text-white/40 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-mono">
              Live
            </span>
          </div>
          <button
            onClick={fetchDiagnostics}
            disabled={isRefreshingDiag}
            className="p-1 rounded bg-[#121217] text-white/45 hover:text-[#e8a838] transition-all hover:bg-white/5 flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] font-sans"
            title="Refresh Server Telemetry Metrics"
          >
            <RefreshCw className={`w-3 h-3 ${isRefreshingDiag ? "animate-spin text-[#e8a838]" : ""}`} />
            Refresh Log
          </button>
        </div>

        {isDemoMode ? (
          <div className="p-3 bg-amber-500/5 border border-amber-500/10 rounded-lg flex items-start gap-2.5">
            <AlertTriangle className="w-4 h-4 text-[#e8a838] flex-shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
            <div className="text-[11px] text-white/60 leading-relaxed font-sans">
              <strong className="text-white font-medium">Demo Mode Simulation is currently enabled.</strong> Real-time hardware diagnostics, bridge signals, and script evaluations are currently mocked using client state parameters. Toggle indices inside the header bar to engage live TCP operations.
            </div>
          </div>
        ) : diagnostics ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
            {/* Bento stats row */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-2">
              <div className="bg-[#121217] p-2.5 rounded-lg border border-white/5">
                <span className="text-[9px] text-white/30 uppercase tracking-widest font-mono block">Node / Engine</span>
                <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-white/80 font-mono mt-1 block truncate">
                  {diagnostics.nodeVersion || "Unknown"}
                </span>
              </div>
              <div className="bg-[#121217] p-2.5 rounded-lg border border-white/5">
                <span className="text-[9px] text-white/30 uppercase tracking-widest font-mono block">Uniques Handshakes</span>
                <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-white/80 font-mono mt-1 block">
                  WS: {diagnostics.metrics.browserWebSocketConnectionsCount} | TCP: {diagnostics.metrics.aeTcpConnectionsCount}
                </span>
              </div>
              <div className="bg-[#121217] p-2.5 rounded-lg border border-white/5">
                <span className="text-[9px] text-white/30 uppercase tracking-widest font-mono block">Commands Run</span>
                <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-emerald-400 font-mono mt-1 block">
                  Success: {diagnostics.metrics.commandsResolved}
                </span>
              </div>
              <div className="bg-[#121217] p-2.5 rounded-lg border border-white/5">
                <span className="text-[9px] text-white/30 uppercase tracking-widest font-mono block">Errors / Timeouts</span>
                <span className="text-xs font-semibold text-rose-400 font-mono mt-1 block">
                  Failed: {diagnostics.metrics.commandsFailed} | Overtime: {diagnostics.metrics.commandsTimedOut}
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Diagnostics advisory check list */}
            <div className="flex flex-col lg:flex-row gap-3">
              {/* Files Check List */}
              <div className="flex-1 bg-[#121217] p-3 rounded-lg border border-white/5 flex flex-col gap-1.5">
                <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white/40 uppercase tracking-widest mb-1 font-mono flex items-center gap-1">
                  <Cpu className="w-3 h-3 text-[#e8a838]" /> System File Calibration
                </span>
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-[11px] font-sans">
                  <span className="text-white/60">package.json metadata</span>
                  <span className="font-mono text-[10px] text-emerald-400 flex items-center gap-1">
                    <CheckCircle className="w-3 h-3 text-emerald-400" /> CALIBRATED
                  </span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-[11px] font-sans">
                  <span className="text-white/60">bridge.jsx auto-generation</span>
                  <span className="font-mono text-[10px] text-emerald-400 flex items-center gap-1">
                    <CheckCircle className="w-3 h-3 text-emerald-400" /> DEPLOYED
                  </span>
                </div>
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-[11px] font-sans">
                  <span className="text-white/60">diagnostics logging module</span>
                  <span className="font-mono text-[10px] text-emerald-400 flex items-center gap-1">
                    <CheckCircle className="w-3 h-3 text-emerald-400" /> ACTIVE
                  </span>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Errors report section */}
              <div className="flex-[1.5] bg-[#070709] border border-white/5 rounded-lg p-3 overflow-hidden max-h-[120px] overflow-y-auto">
                <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white/40 uppercase tracking-widest mb-1.5 font-mono flex items-center gap-1 block">
                  <Shield className="w-3 h-3 text-rose-400" /> Unique Error Capture (Deduplicated)
                </span>
                {diagnostics.errors && diagnostics.errors.length > 0 ? (
                  <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
                    {diagnostics.errors.map((err: any, idx: number) => (
                      <div key={idx} className="border-l-2 border-rose-500 pl-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-mono leading-relaxed">
                        <div className="text-white/80 font-bold truncate">({err.type.toUpperCase()}) {err.message}</div>
                        {err.details && <div className="text-rose-400/70 truncate">{err.details}</div>}
                        <div className="text-[8px] text-white/30">Occurrences: {err.count} | Last error: {new Date(err.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString()}</div>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <div className="text-[11px] text-emerald-400 flex items-center gap-1.5 py-2 font-sans font-medium">
                    <CheckCircle className="w-4 h-4 text-emerald-400" /> All systems building, transmitting, and responding flawlessly! No errors recorded in telemetry cache.
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <div className="text-[11px] text-white/40 font-sans italic text-center py-2">
            Loading real-time platform telemetry diagnostics...
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

  };
};

export interface Layer {
  index: number;
  name: string;
  enabled: boolean;
  locked: boolean;
  solo: boolean;
  shy: boolean;
  threeDLayer?: boolean; // mapping threeDLayer in JSX
  threeD?: boolean; // local normalized
  hasVideo?: boolean;
  hasAudio?: boolean;
  startTime?: number;
  inPoint?: number;
  outPoint?: number;
  layerType: 'text' | 'shape' | 'camera' | 'light' | 'null' | 'solid' | 'av' | 'unknown' | string;
  selected: boolean;
  parentIndex: number | null;
  stretch: number;
  blendMode?: string;
  motionBlur?: boolean;
  adjustmentLayer?: boolean;
  collapseTransformations?: boolean;
}

export interface CompSettings {
  width: number;
  height: number;
  frameRate: number;
  duration: number;
  bgColor: [number, number, number];
  motionBlur: boolean;
  hideShyLayers?: boolean;
  name: string;
}

export interface EffectProperty {
  index: number;
  name: string;
  matchName: string;
  propertyType: number;
  isGroup: boolean;
  value?: any;
  isTimeVarying?: boolean;
  numKeys?: number;
  canSetExpression?: boolean;
  properties?: EffectProperty[];
}

export interface Effect {
  index: number;
  name: string;
  matchName: string;
  properties?: EffectProperty[];
}

export interface Mask {
  index: number;
  name: string;
  maskMode: 'ADD' | 'SUBTRACT' | 'INTERSECT' | 'LIGHTEN' | 'DARKEN' | 'DIFFERENCE' | 'NONE' | string;
  inverted: boolean;
  maskFeather: number | number[];
  maskOpacity: number;
  maskExpansion: number;
}

export interface Keyframe {
  index: number;
  time: number;
  value: any;
}

export interface CompItem {
  index: number;
  id: number;
  name: string;
  width: number;
  height: number;
  duration: number;
  frameRate: number;
  numLayers: number;
}

FILE: src/utils.ts

export function rgbToHex(r: number, g: number, b: number): string {
  const pad = (x: number) => x.toString(16).padStart(2, "0");
  return "#" + pad(r) + pad(g) + pad(b);
}

export function hexToRgb(hex: string): { r: number; g: number; b: number } {
  const cleanHex = hex.replace("#", "");
  return {
    r: parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16) || 0,
    g: parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16) || 0,
    b: parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16) || 0,
  };
}

export function formatTimecode(time: number, fps: number): string {
  const totalFrames = Math.round(time * fps);
  const h = Math.floor(time / 3600);
  const m = Math.floor((time % 3600) / 60);
  const s = Math.floor(time % 60);
  const f = totalFrames % Math.round(fps);
  
  const pad = (n: number) => String(n).padStart(2, "0");
  return `${pad(h)}:${pad(m)}:${pad(s)}:${pad(f)}`;
}

export function esc(s: string): string {
  return String(s)
    .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
    .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
    .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
    .replace(/"/g, "&quot;")
    .replace(/'/g, "&#039;");
}


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: src/utils/bridgeScript.ts
------------------------------------------------------------

/**
 * Exports the raw string content of the bridge.jsx script
 * for direct, foolproof client-side downloading in the UI.
 */
export const BRIDGE_JSX_CONTENT = `/**
 * AFTER EFFECTS TO TOUCHTOOLS TCP BRIDGE SCRIPT (NON-BLOCKING)
 * 
 * Instructions:
 * 1. Open Adobe After Effects.
 * 2. Ensure "Allow Scripts to Write Files and Access Network" is enabled:
 *    Preferences > Scripting & Expressions > Check "Allow Scripts to Write Files and Access Network"
 * 3. Go to File > Scripts > Run Script File... and choose this bridge.jsx.
 * 4. This runs in the background (non-blocking). After Effects remains fully active and interactive!
 */

var TouchToolsBridge = {
    host: "127.0.0.1",
    port: 8092,
    socket: null,
    taskId: null,
    buffer: "",
    isActive: false,
    lastConnectAttempt: 0,
    isOpen: false, // Explicit connection state tracking flag since ExtendScript Socket lacks 'connected' property
    
    connect: function() {
        if (this.socket) {
            try { this.socket.close(); } catch(e) {}
        }
        
        var s = new Socket();
        s.timeout = 0; // Set socket timeout to 0 (non-blocking)
        
        $.writeln("TouchTools: Connecting to " + this.host + ":" + this.port + "...");
        
        if (!s.open(this.host + ":" + this.port, "UTF-8")) {
            $.writeln("TouchTools: Handshake connection failed. Standby mode active.");
            this.isOpen = false;
            return false;
        }
        
        this.socket = s;
        this.socket.timeout = 0; // ensure non-blocking read
        this.isOpen = true;
        
        $.writeln("TouchTools: Connected successfully!");
        
        // Handshake
        this.socket.write(JSON.stringify({
            type: "status",
            status: "connected",
            message: "After Effects is hooked up and ready"
        }) + "\\n");
        
        this.buffer = "";
        return true;
    },
    
    poll: function() {
        // Auto-reconnect if socket drops - throttled to every 5000ms to preserve After Effects performance!
        if (!this.isOpen || !this.socket) {
            var now = new Date().getTime();
            if (now - this.lastConnectAttempt < 5000) {
                return; // Delay retry so we do not freeze After Effects
            }
            this.lastConnectAttempt = now;
            $.writeln("TouchTools: Socket offline. Reconnecting...");
            if (!this.connect()) {
                return;
            }
        }
        
        try {
            if (this.socket.connected === false) {
                throw new Error("closed");
            }

            // Direct immediate read of any waiting buffer characters (non-blocking)
            var data = this.socket.read();
            
            // Check for termination / empty responses and actual closed signals
            if (data === null || data === "") {
                // On some systems socket.read() returns "" or null when empty but still connected.
                // We verify socket health with write("") fallback and the connected property.
                if (this.socket.connected === false) {
                    throw new Error("closed");
                }
                try {
                    this.socket.write("");
                    if (this.socket.error && this.socket.error.indexOf("closed") !== -1) {
                        throw new Error("closed");
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                    throw new Error("closed");
                }
            } else if (this.socket.error && this.socket.error.indexOf("closed") !== -1) {
                throw new Error("closed");
            }
            
            if (data && data.length > 0) {
                this.buffer += data;
                var lines = this.buffer.split("\\n");
                this.buffer = lines.pop(); // save incomplete line
                
                for (var i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
                    var line = lines[i].replace(/^\\s+|\\s+$/g, '');
                    if (line === '') continue;
                    
                    try {
                        var cmd = JSON.parse(line);
                        this.handleCommand(cmd);
                    } catch (e) {
                        $.writeln("TouchTools: JSON parse/exec error: " + e.toString());
                    }
                }
            }
        } catch (err) {
            $.writeln("TouchTools: Read error: " + err.toString());
            this.isOpen = false;
            try { this.socket.close(); } catch (e) {}
            this.socket = null;
        }
    },
    
    handleCommand: function(cmd) {
        if (!cmd.id) return;
        
        var resultStr = "";
        var isError = false;
        
        try {
            if (cmd.action === "executeScript") {
                var value = eval(cmd.script);
                resultStr = value !== undefined ? String(value) : "undefined";
            } else if (cmd.action === "addSolid") {
                var activeComp = app.project.activeItem;
                if (activeComp && activeComp instanceof CompItem) {
                    var layer = activeComp.layers.addSolid(
                        cmd.color || [1, 1, 1],
                        cmd.name || "Solid Layer",
                        cmd.width || activeComp.width,
                        cmd.height || activeComp.height,
                        activeComp.pixelAspect,
                        activeComp.duration
                    );
                    resultStr = "Created solid layer: " + layer.name;
                } else {
                    throw new Error("No active composition found selection.");
                }
            } else if (cmd.action === "addText") {
                var activeComp = app.project.activeItem;
                if (activeComp && activeComp instanceof CompItem) {
                    var layer = activeComp.layers.addText(cmd.text || "TouchTools Text");
                    resultStr = "Created text layer: " + layer.name;
                } else {
                    throw new Error("No active composition found selection.");
                }
            } else if (cmd.action === "addShape") {
                var activeComp = app.project.activeItem;
                if (activeComp && activeComp instanceof CompItem) {
                    var layer = activeComp.layers.addShape();
                    layer.name = cmd.name || "Shape Layer";
                    resultStr = "Created shape layer: " + layer.name;
                } else {
                    throw new Error("No active composition found.");
                }
            } else if (cmd.action === "updateTransform") {
                var activeComp = app.project.activeItem;
                if (activeComp && activeComp instanceof CompItem) {
                    var layer = activeComp.layer(cmd.layerIndex);
                    if (layer) {
                        if (cmd.position) {
                            layer.property("ADBE Transform Group").property("ADBE Position").setValue(cmd.position);
                        }
                        if (cmd.scale) {
                            layer.property("ADBE Transform Group").property("ADBE Scale").setValue([cmd.scale, cmd.scale, 100]);
                        }
                        if (cmd.opacity !== undefined) {
                            layer.property("ADBE Transform Group").property("ADBE Opacity").setValue(cmd.opacity);
                        }
                        resultStr = "Updated layer properties";
                    } else {
                        throw new Error("Layer not found at index: " + cmd.layerIndex);
                    }
                } else {
                    throw new Error("No active composition found.");
                }
            } else if (cmd.action === "setValue") {
                // EXTREMELY IMPORTANT: direct property values from interactive slider components
                var activeComp = app.project.activeItem;
                if (activeComp && activeComp instanceof CompItem) {
                    var layer = activeComp.layer(cmd.layerIndex);
                    if (layer) {
                        var prop = layer;
                        if (cmd.propertyGroup) {
                            prop = prop.property(cmd.propertyGroup);
                        }
                        if (prop && cmd.propertyPath) {
                            prop = prop.property(cmd.propertyPath);
                        }
                        if (prop && typeof prop.setValue === "function") {
                            prop.setValue(cmd.value);
                            resultStr = "Set property value successfully";
                        } else {
                            throw new Error("Property path not settable or missing");
                        }
                    } else {
                        throw new Error("Layer not found at index: " + cmd.layerIndex);
                    }
                } else {
                    throw new Error("No active composition found.");
                }
            } else {
                throw new Error("Unknown action: " + cmd.action);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            resultStr = e.toString();
            isError = true;
        }
        
        var response = {
            id: cmd.id,
            type: isError ? "error" : "result",
            result: isError ? null : resultStr,
            error: isError ? resultStr : null
        };
        
        try {
            this.socket.write(JSON.stringify(response) + "\\n");
            if (this.socket.error) {
                $.writeln("TouchTools: Write error registered: " + this.socket.error);
                this.isOpen = false;
            }
        } catch (err) {
            $.writeln("TouchTools: Write response failed: " + err.toString());
            this.isOpen = false;
        }
    },
    
    stop: function() {
        if (this.taskId) {
            try { app.cancelTask(this.taskId); } catch(e) {}
            this.taskId = null;
        }
        if (this.socket) {
            try { this.socket.close(); } catch(e) {}
            this.socket = null;
        }
        this.isActive = false;
        $.writeln("TouchTools: Background Scheduler Cleared.");
    },
    
    start: function() {
        this.stop();
        this.connect();
        this.isActive = true;
        // Schedule poll checks every 40ms without freezing After Effects!
        this.taskId = app.scheduleTask("TouchToolsBridge.poll();", 40, true);
        $.writeln("TouchTools: Non-blocking client started in background container.");
    }
};

// Simple, syntax-error free JSON Shim for older ExtendScript contexts
if (typeof JSON !== "object") {
    JSON = {
        parse: function(str) { return eval("(" + str + ")"); },
        stringify: function(obj) {
            var t = typeof (obj);
            if (t !== "object" || obj === null) {
                if (t === "string") return '"' + obj.replace(/"/g, '\\\\"') + '"';
                return String(obj);
            } else {
                var json = [], arr = (obj && obj.constructor === Array);
                for (var n in obj) {
                    var v = obj[n], vt = typeof(v);
                    if (vt === "string") v = '"' + v.replace(/"/g, '\\\\"') + '"';
                    else if (vt === "object" && v !== null) v = JSON.stringify(v);
                    json.push((arr ? "" : '"' + n + '":') + String(v));
                }
                return (arr ? "[" : "{") + String(json) + (arr ? "]" : "}");
            }
        }
    };
}

TouchToolsBridge.start();
`;

@echo off
title TouchTools Quickstart Setup
echo ==========================================
echo       TouchTools Quickstart Protocol
echo ==========================================
echo.
echo [1/3] Checking environment utilities...
node -v >nul 2>&1
if %errorlevel% neq 0 (
    echo [ERROR] Node.js is not installed on this system.
    echo Please download and install Node.js from https://nodejs.org/ first!
    pause
    exit /b
)

:: Ensure we are starting in the folder containing this batch script
cd /d "%~dp0"

echo [2/3] Checking and installing dependencies (npm install)...
if not exist node_modules (
    echo No node_modules folder detected. Running initial package assembly...
    call npm install
) else (
    echo Dependencies already mapped. Continuing...
)

echo [3/3] Initiating full-stack development workspace...
echo.
echo ==================================================
echo TouchTools will boot at http://localhost:3000
echo Auto-generating 'bridge.jsx' in this folder...
echo ==================================================
echo.

:: Automatically pop open the browser to the interface
start http://localhost:3000

:: Run development sequence
call npm run dev
pause


------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: start.sh
------------------------------------------------------------

#!/bin/bash
clear
echo "=========================================="
echo "      TouchTools Quickstart Protocol"
echo "=========================================="
echo ""

# Ensure script runs from the directory it is hosted in
cd "$(dirname "$0")"

# 1. Inspect Node
if ! command -v node &> /dev/null
then
    echo "[ERROR] Node.js is not installed. Please download it from https://nodejs.org/ before running."
    exit 1
fi

# 2. Map dependencies
echo "[1/3] Checking and installing dependencies..."
if [ ! -d "node_modules" ]; then
    echo "No node_modules detected. Running initial package assembly..."
    npm install
else
    echo "Dependencies already mapped. Continuing..."
fi

# 3. Boot workspace
echo "[2/3] Preparing workspace assets..."
echo "Auto-generating 'bridge.jsx' in this folder..."
echo ""
echo "=================================================="
echo "TouchTools will boot at http://localhost:3000"
echo "=================================================="
echo ""

# Try opening localhost in default browser
if [ "$(uname)" == "Darwin" ]; then
    open http://localhost:3000
elif [ "$(expr substr $(uname -s) 1 5)" == "Linux" ]; then
    xdg-open http://localhost:3000 &> /dev/null &
fi

npm run dev

import tailwindcss from '@tailwindcss/vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';
import path from 'path';
import {defineConfig} from 'vite';

export default defineConfig(() => {
  return {
    plugins: [react(), tailwindcss()],
    resolve: {
      alias: {
        '@': path.resolve(__dirname, '.'),
      },
    },
    server: {
      // HMR is disabled in AI Studio via DISABLE_HMR env var.
      // Do not modifyâfile watching is disabled to prevent flickering during agent edits.
      hmr: process.env.DISABLE_HMR !== 'true',
      // Disable file watching when DISABLE_HMR is true to save CPU during agent edits.
      watch: process.env.DISABLE_HMR === 'true' ? null : {
        ignored: [
          '**/touchtools-diagnostics.json',
          '**/touchtools-diagnostics.log',
          '**/bridge.jsx',
          '**/config.json',
          '**/*.log',
          '**/*.json'
        ]
      },
    },
  };
});
